saṃtarpayām āsa yataḥ sa lokaṃ dānāmbubhiḥ sasyam ivāmbugarbhaḥ । tato mahāmegha iti kṣitīśo yathārthanāmātiśayo babhūva ।। na tasya rājyadyutivistareṣu vyāsaktadīnaṃ hṛdayaṃ babhūva । anarthabhūtān sa parārtham arthān drumaḥ phalānīva babhāra sādhuḥ ।।
babhūva tasmin pitarīva loko viśrambhasaṃbhogasukhapragalbhaḥ । suteṣv iva premanibaddhabhāvo babhūva so api kṣitipaḥ prajāsu ।। sagauravo asau guruṣu prakṛtyā dīneṣu kāruṇyamṛdusvabhāvaḥ । kṛtāparādheṣv api maitracittaḥ samantabhadras tu suhṛjjaneṣu ।।
babhūva tasya graharājakīrtes tathāgraho na svaparigraheṣu । yathā tadīyāsu mamatvam āsīj janasya saṃpatsv atiśāyinīṣu ।। jagrāha dānena sa kāṃś cid eva priyābhidhānair aparān vicitraiḥ । tathārthacaryābhir anarthabhīruḥ kāṃś cit samānārthatayārthabhūtaḥ ।।
yan nātmasāc ca naralokapatiś cakāra । lokeṣv asaṃstutasuhṛd bhagavān babhūva ।। sa kadā cin mahīpatir amātyagaṇapuraskṛta udaṅmukho dadarśātasīkusumarāśisaṃkāśam ākāśam avagāhya patato bhagavataḥ pratyekabuddhān paramavismitamanā hy amātyān abravīt ।। paśyantu bhavantaḥ ।। ete kaṣāyaparuṣāmbarasaṃvṛtāṅgā vyomātasīkusumarāśinibhaṃ vigāhya ।
āyānti ke apy upaśamastimitapracārā bhūrjadrumā iva marudbhir udastamūlāḥ ।। anyatamo apy amātyaḥ sasaṃbhramo abravīt ।। samyag abhihitaṃ devena kutaḥ ।। āyānty amī kāñcanarāśigaurā vidhūtakāṣāyapaṭāntabhaṅgāḥ । parasparāsliṣṭavikīrṇapakṣāḥ khaṃ cakravākā iva śobhayantaḥ ।।
aparo apy āha ।। svacchendranīlopalarāgam ete nabhaḥ samutpatya samāpatanti । samīryamāṇāḥ pavanena saṃdhyākalaṅkitāntāḥ śaradīva meghāḥ ।। upaśamaramaṇīye cāpatanti prakṛtyā ।
na ca gaganam asaṅgaṃ pādasaṃcārayogyaṃ ।। yathā yathā te nikaṭī bhavanti vratīśvarāḥ śāntim ivākirantaḥ । tathā tathā vismayaharṣapūrṇā rājanvatī sā samitiś cakampe ।। atṛptā eva te teṣāṃ darśanena mahātmanāṃ ।
babhūvur atha cātīyus teṣāṃ nayanagocaraṃ ।। atha sa pārthivas teṣāṃ maharṣīṇāṃ darśanenāvarjitamanās tān amātyān abravīt ।। idam āścāryam ālokya kautūhalasamākulaṃ । mano mama tad icchāmi śrotum eṣāṃ pravistaraṃ ।।
atha teṣāṃ nṛpatisacivānām abhijñātataro amātyas taṃ rājānam abravīt ।। śrūyatāṃ mahārāja ।। notpadyante yadā buddhā bhagavantaḥ kṛpātmakāḥ । apāsya rajasāṃ vṛttiṃ dīrghakālānuśāyinīm ।। āvṛte tamasā loke samantād aparāyaṇe ।
bhavaty eṣāṃ tadā janma janmaparyantagāmināṃ ।। pratītyotpādagāmbhīryadūrānugatabuddhayaḥ । prāptaśayyāsanaratā hīnadīnānukampakāḥ ।। saṃsargabhīravo nityaṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvaparāyaṇāḥ ।
vicaranti jagaty ete jaṅgamāḥ puṇyarāśayaḥ ।। ātmānam ekaṃ praty ete buddhā yasmād ataḥ kila । pratyekabuddhā ity evaṃ pratimānam upāgatāḥ ।। atha sa rājā sutarāṃ tadguṇākṛṣṭahṛdayaḥ sa tam amātyam abravīt ।। atha kutrāmī bhagavantaḥ prativasantīti ।। sa prāha ।।
meghasya rājño vijite jitātman vasanty amī dagdhabhavādhivāsāḥ । himādrikuñjeṣu namannamerupratānasaṃsaktamahīruheṣu ।। rājovāca ।। asti kaś cid upāyo yenāmī madviṣayāntam āvaseyur ity amātyo abravīt ।। asti mahārāja yadi megharājā prārthyate tadanvabhyarthitāḥ kilāmī tvadviṣayam alaṃ kurvantyaḥ prāpnuvanti ceti ।। atha bodhisattvaḥ puṇyeṣv ādaropadarśanārtham amātyān āha ।। tena hi bhavantaḥ sajjīkuruta ।। tadanurūpamānapātraṃ svayam evāhaṃ gatvā meghaṃ rājānam asminn arthe vijñāpayiṣyāmīty adhvasaṃbhrāntās te puruṣā bodhisattvam āhuḥ ।। nārhati devo dūtamātrasādhye prayojane khedam āpattum ।। ājñāsukharasaṃ rājyam anekāpāyasaṃkaṭaṃ ।
pararāṣṭram ato gantuṃ sahasā tava na kṣamaṃ ।। bodhisattvo abravīt ।। svahite apy abhiyuktānāṃ karuṇāvikalātmanāṃ । khedaḥ kaḥ puṇyakāmānāṃ bhavādhvaparivartināṃ ।।
ātmatvenaiva yair eva tad upāttaṃ bhavatrayaṃ । jagadatyantabandhūnāṃ teṣāṃ khedaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।। na ca kāryābhiniṣpattir dūtasādhyā garīyasī । nāsmād gurutaraṃ cāsti karaṇīyaṃ mama paraṃ ।।
na cājñārabhasārambhe na rājyabhāraṃ vahāmy ahaṃ । jagatāṃ vayam eveha kṛpayā kiṃkarāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। anekāpāyasaṃrāddhaṃ rājyaṃ yenaiva bhūbhṛtāṃ । tenaivāsya kṣamas tyāgaḥ kupitasyeva bhoginaḥ ।।
dharmād eva ca saṃprāpya rājyaśrīsukhasaṃpadaḥ । audāsīnyaṃ kathaṃ nāma kuryāt tatraiva paṇḍitaḥ ।। api ca bhadantaḥ ।। vinā śramais tuccham asāram adhruvaṃ sukhaṃ na kāmāśrayam apy avāpyate ।
aśeṣalokatrayasaṃpadāspadaṃ padaṃ kim aṅgāpratimasvayaṃbhuvāṃ ।। niveśya kāmeṣu caleṣu mānasaṃ mudhaiva khinnā vayam anyajanmasu । jagaddhitāya tv adhunābhivāñchitā bhavantu nas tv antakarāḥ pariśramāḥ ।। kathaṃ nu tasmin na yateta buddhimān nibadhya yasminn abhilāṣamātrakaṃ ।
asaṃstutānām api caikabandhutāṃ jano janānām upayāti tatkṣaṇāt ।। tadatyayāśaṅkibhiś cāmātyaiḥ sa mahātmā punaḥ punaḥ pratibodhyamāno api naiva teṣāṃ vacanaṃ pramāṇayām āsa ।। tyaktaspṛhatvāt kṣitipasya tasya sarvatra kāruṇyamayī pravṛttiḥ । guṇānurāgāt sa tathāpi teṣāṃ pūjāṃ munīnāṃ prati sādaro abhūt ।।
guṇodgatā eva guṇoditeṣu bhavanti pūjāpratipattinamrāḥ । ya eva ratnātiśayāntarajñās ta eva teṣv atyadhikaṃ yatante ।। phalābhilāṣopahatāntarātmā parīkṣate pātraviśeṣam eva । kṛpālukas tv arthitayaiva tuṣṭaḥ pravartate yācanakeṣu sāraṃ ।।
vanaspatīnām iva janma yeṣāṃ paropakāraikarasasvabhāvaṃ । labheta teṣāṃ hṛdaye avakāśaṃ khalā phalāśā viduṣāṃ kathaṃ ca ।। atha sa mahāsattvo guṇānuvṛttisthirānurāgeṇa mahatā balena parivṛtaḥ svapuravarād viniryayau ।। nirgacchantaṃ cainaṃ dūrvāpravālakusumaphalavyagrātyucchritaikapāṇayo dvijavarā jaya jaya mahārājety uccair ānandayām āsuḥ ।। atha sa mahātmā laukikamaṅgalāpariniṣpattim abhiprakāśayan buddhānām eva ca bhagavatāṃ guṇānuvādaṃ maṅgalaṃ codbhāvayan vyāpinā svareṇa tān amaṅgale maṅgalābhiniveśino viprān abravīt ।। sarvānarthopasaṃhārapragalbhaiḥ kleśaśatrubhiḥ ।
parājitānāṃ ko nāma vijayaḥ klībacetasāṃ ।। tṛṣṇāvallīṃ samūlāṃ bhavataruśikharārohinīṃ yo dadāha । lokālokasvabhāvaḥ sa jayati bhagavān bhagnasaṃsāracakraḥ ।। duṣpūraṃ viṣayābhilāṣakṛpaṇaṃ māyāsvabhāvaṃ calaṃ ।
yaś cittaṃ damayāṃ babhūva sa jayatv avyagracetā muniḥ ।। akliṣṭām api nirdadhāva nivṛtiṃ kālatrayavyāpinīṃ । prajñānaṃ bhagavān asau vijayate buddho jagacchaṅkaraḥ ।। sa krameṇa vyatītya tālahiṃtālatamālanaktamālaniculabakulakānanopaśobhitaṃ svaviṣayam khadirabadarabilveṅgudaśamīpalāśagahanadurgām aṭavīṃ prapede ।। tasya khalu mahāsattvasya puṇyatarṣeṇa drutataraṃ vrajataḥ ।।
niruddhaṃ khaṃ reje pulinam iva paryastam udadheḥ । jalair nāgendrāṇāṃ navatamavanīhārapaṭalaiḥ ।। so atikramya tām aṭavīm anukrameṇa meghasya rājño viṣayam anuprāptaḥ । tadāgamanasaṃbhrāntaś ca megho mahīpatir viditatadguṇaprabhāvaḥ pratyudgamyainaṃ sabahumānapraharṣavismayavikacalocano mahatā satkāreṇa mānayitvā mahārhāsanopaviṣṭaṃ tat tat priyam avocat ।। susvāgataṃ kṣitīndrāya dhanyam āgamanaṃ tava ।
subhāṣitam idaṃ loke jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyasi ।। ko nu saṃbhāvayet puṇyāṃ pramodāmṛtapeśalāṃ । āvayoḥ saṃgatim imāṃ himavadvindhyayor iva ।। dṛśyase caritair eva kāmaṃ lokāntacāribhiḥ ।
sākṣād vo darśanaṃ yat tu tan maṅgalyaphalodayaṃ ।। pratyakṣam api kalyāṇaṃ manorathavidūragaṃ । na śraddhatte janaḥ prāyaḥ prītipreṅkholitāśayaḥ ।। svapno ayam uta māyeti niścayaṃ na labhāmahe ।
bhavantam api paśyanto locanānandabāndhavaṃ ।। kac cid aklāntakāyas tvaṃ rājan kac cid anāmayaḥ । kac cid viśrambhaniḥsaṅgaḥ praṇayābhimukho mayi ।। kac cin notkaṇṭhayanti tvāṃ daksiṇāpathacandrikāḥ ।
pradhyānastimitātāmraparyantanayanāḥ priyāḥ ।। anapāyī bhavet kac cid ayatnaḥ satsamāgamaḥ । kac cid atrābhiramase svadeśa iva bhūpate ।। atha bodhisattvas taṃ rājānam amlānapraṇayaśībharair vacobhiḥ samuttejayann abravīt ।।
dṛṣṭvaiva darśanīyaṃ tvāṃ viśrānto ahaṃ mahīpate । anāryasyāpi viśrambhaḥ kasya na syād bhavādṛśe ।। tvayy asaṃstutasadbandhau bāndhave purataḥ sthite । kiṃ cānyad vallabhataraṃ mamotkaṇṭhānibandhanaṃ ।।
viditāś ca mahārāja mama priyasamāgamāḥ । vitathālpasukhāsvādavyasanāyāsahetavaḥ ।। ye arthāḥ svapne anubhūyante ye ca nidrāparikṣaye । tesāṃ nirbhuktimuktānāṃ viśeṣo nopalabhyate ।।
svapnamāyopamāneṣu muhūrtapariṇāmiṣu । prasaṅgaṃ matimān kuryān na priyapraṇayeṣv ataḥ ।। priyo mamety evam anādikālapravṛttam udvṛttam analpagarbhaṃ । sukhābhidhānaṃ pravadanti duḥkhaṃ vyatītaduḥkhā munayaḥ purāṇāḥ ।।
kṛpā kṛpāvastuṣu saṃpratāryate striyaḥ kṛpāvastu viśeṣataḥ satāṃ । ato matir me karuṇānupātinī priyāsu rājan na tu vibhramāturā ।। svabhāvadīnāḥ paratantravṛttayaḥ sadāturā matsaramānamanmathaiḥ । pathi prakīrṇā iva māṃsapeśikāḥ kathaṃ nu na syuḥ pramadāḥ kṛpāspadaṃ ।।
atha sa rājā prasāditamānasas tair bodhisattvavacanakusumaiḥ praṇamyainam abravīt ।। ājñāpaya mahārāja yatra māṃ manyase kṣamaṃ । bhavadvidhānāṃ kṛtyeṣu vayam ānamramūrtayaḥ ।। prasannamānasaṃ sa cainam avetya bodhisattvaḥ saṃpraharṣayann abravīt ।।
tavaiva saphalaṃ janma sujīvaṃ tvaṃ ca jīvasi । aiśvaryaṃ tava pātrasthaṃ yathārthā śrīs tavaiva ca ।। yas tvam eṣāṃ bhagavatāṃ bhavasaṃbhogavidviṣāṃ । satkāravyapadeśena tanoṣi yaśasā jagat ।।
suhṛdaḥ saṃvibhajyante dārair api dhanair api । saṃvibhāgas tu dharmeṇa durlabho bhuvi nāsti vā ।। dharmātithyam ato rājan mama tvaṃ kartum arhasi । na hi saṃbhāvanā satsu dṛṣṭā vandhyaphalodayā ।।
svargo mokṣaḥ sukhāny arthā dharmād eva yaśāṃsi ca । dadhad dharmam ato yuṅkte svargamokṣasukhādibhiḥ ।। saddharmapraguṇaṃ mitraṃ karaṇīyaṃ balād api । eṣaiva suhṛdāṃ loke sādhoḥ sādhīyasī sthitiḥ ।।
atithir mitram arthīva satkārāyatanaṃ paraṃ mayi caitat trayaṃ yasmād ato me abhyarthanāṃ kuru ।। sravann iva prasādas te lakṣyate mukhapaṅkajāt । puṇyasaṃbhogavātsalyam udgiraṃl lakṣyase girā ।। anujñātā tvayā rājann ime praksīṇakalmaṣāḥ ।
vasantu dakṣiṇīyāgryā dakṣiṇāpathabhūmiṣu ।। athāsau mahīpatir bodhisattvam abravīt ।। śakye tat kuśalaṃ dātuṃ svasaṃtānagataṃ yadi । dadyāṃ tad api suvyaktaṃ bhavate kṛtavedine ।।
vayaṃ rājyaṃ ca dātāro yad vānyat sādhu manyase । tathaiva prabhutāṃ tatra nāvagantavyam anyathā ।। mayā yat puṇyam āryāṇām eṣām apaciteś citaṃ । tvadabhyāgamanākālakaumudī tat kṛtaiva me ।।
mitram ekāntakalyāṇaṃ bandhur atyantavatsalaḥ । guṇavān dakṣiṇīyas tvaṃ nāthaś cānuttaro mama ।। kṣudrasattvo api ko nāma tvadājñām abhilaṅghayet । draṣṭavyaratnaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca na prasīded bhavādṛśaṃ ।।
ekaṃ tv atra mahārāja vaidhuram avagacchāmi । yena me vaktum asty etān maharṣīn asmin prayojane saṃkucati mānasam ।। ete hi mahātmāno vivekaratipriyatvād abhiramante himavati śailarāje ।। paśya mahārāja ।। amī hi himavatprasthāḥ kadalīkhaṇśamaṇḍitāḥ । vivekāyaiva sādhūnāṃ śaṅkhadhātrā vinirmitāḥ ।। hariṇā luñcitopāntaśādvalaśyāmanirjharān । devadārudrumān paśya kūṭāgārān ivodgatān ।।
khyāpayantīva lokānāṃ vinipātaṃ himāpagāḥ । taraṅgaiḥ kūlapāṣāṇabhidyamānair muhur muhuḥ ।। etāḥ snigdhacchadacchāyāḥ padmakadrumarājayaḥ । yatīn āśvāsayantīva saṃsārodvignamānasān ।।
klāntānāṃ vratinām eṣa svedabindūn apohate । prāleyakaṇasaṃparkaśiśiro vanamārutaḥ ।। upatyakāḥ padmakapuṣpapāṭalāḥ śilīndhrakāpādapavāritātapāḥ । imā himādre ramayanti mānasaṃ nivṛttasaṃrāgaviṣaṃ vipaścitāṃ ।।
himācalasyopanitambarohiṇāṃ nirīkṣamāṇāḥ saralāśikhāvatāṃ । vanāni cetaḥsthitim āpnuvanty amī sumedhasaḥ kāmavivekapeśalāṃ ।। bodhisattvaḥ provāca ।। timiradrumasaṃchannā viviktābhogakandarāḥ ।
tatrāpy anuguṇā santi velāśailaḥ prahāṇināṃ ।। tālahintālamālinyaḥ sarito haritopalāḥ । santi tatrāpi hārītapakṣavikṣobhitormayaḥ ।। taraṅginīnām upakaṇṭharohiṇāṃ palāśinām puṣpabharāturāḥ śikhāḥ ।
vidhūya tatrāpi yatīn niṣevate samudravelājalaśītalo anilaḥ ।। sarasamaricavallīśyāmarodho vanasya dhvanir acalasuruṅgāmurcchito apy amburāśeḥ । aviralaparipāto abhyāsayogānupātī sthirayati kila bhikṣos tatra cetaḥsamādhiṃ ।। vātāyāsitacandanadrumalatāvikṣiptasūryātapaḥ ।
cetaḥ saṃyaminām alaṃ ramayituṃ śāntaprapañcajvaraṃ ।। śaṣpodbhedais taruṇataruṇaiḥ śyāmaparyantalekhaḥ । vindhyo apy adriḥ praśamamahatāṃ yogināṃ saṃnivāsaḥ ।। niḥśabdākṣaradacchanirjharajalaprakṣālitaprastarāḥ ।
āryāṇām anapāyinīṃ vidadhati pratyātmaveśāṃ ratiṃ ।। tīrāntānatabālavetasataruśreṇīniruddhātapā nadyaḥ svacchajalāntarālavilasanmīnāvalīmekhalāḥ । sakhyaḥ premaniratyayā iva sakhe tatrāpy alaṃ yoginām ākṣeptuṃ viṣayābhilāṣavimukhaṃ pradhyānadhīraṃ manaḥ ।। api ca mahārāja ।। yair adhyastaṃgamitam aśivaṃ skandhasaṃtānabījaṃ ।
lokaṃ teṣāṃ na bhavati mano lokacitrānupāti ।। ye lokārtham anarthabhāravirasaṃ santo vahanty āśrayaṃ । lūtātantuvitānadhūmaśikharaiḥ kāntāravṛkṣaiḥ samāḥ ।। āvir bhavanti tanavo api paropakārā yasmiṃs tad eva ramaṇīyam upaiti sādhuḥ ।
duḥkheṣv anātmasu caleṣv aparāyaṇeṣu kiṃ vā bhaveṣu ratikāraṇam asti rājan ।। svārthānurāgakṛpaṇā matayo narāṇāṃ tucche api vastuni ratiṃ parikalpayanti । utpāda eva mahatāṃ hi jagaddhitāya yeṣāṃ purandarapure api na te ramante ।। prakṛticañcalākulaprasaraṃ yaiś cittam etad vaśīkṛtaṃ ।
ratir udeti nānyatas teṣāṃ adhyātmacintāvihāriṇām ।। ramayanty anuddhṛtavikalpasāyakān saritaḥ sarāṃsi girayo vanāni ca । avikalpagocaravicāriṇo yater vanam eva śāntam iti niścitā matiḥ ।। ajitātmanām anupatanti buddhayo vividhān bahirmukhamanonibandhanān ।
adhicittayogaviduṣāṃ tu yogināṃ atimānuṣe carati gocare matiḥ ।। rajasāṃ vipūyapariṇāhimaṇḍalaṃ paramām avāpya vaśitāṃ svacetasi । anapāyinīm anubhavanti ye ratiṃ bhavanaṃ vanaṃ ca samam eva tān prati ।। viṣayāntarāntaritavibhramaṃ manaḥ praśame rameta katham ity ato yateḥ ।
upadiśyate vanatarupratiśrayo mahatāṃ samaṃ tu viṣayaṃ manaḥsukhaṃ ।। ramaṇīyam etad iti vikṛtaṃ mateḥ pravadanty avandhyavacasaḥ purātanāḥ । kṛtināṃ mano hatavikalpavāsanaṃ na samādhijeṣv api sukheṣu rajyate ।। jagatāṃ hiteṣu caratāṃ mahīpate karuṇaikatānamanasāṃ manasvinām । bhavati vyathātanupariśramais tanor na ca kāyajīvitanikāntividviṣām ।।
gaganopamānamanasāṃ spṛśanty amī na manaḥ sukhārativikalpareṇavaḥ । sukham anyad eva tad apākṛtopamaṃ yad upāsate sukṛtino raṇaṃjahāḥ ।। vratinām adūraparisarpiṇī manaḥsthitir eva nāma jananīva vatsalā । sukham ādadhāti tad atītamānuṣaṃ na marutpater api yad asti vajriṇaḥ ।।
vihatapriyāpriyavikalpavibhramaḥ pṛthivīsamena viharanti cetasā । nṛpa yatra tatra bhavabhoganiḥspṛhā munayo atiśāntasukhamaunalābhinaḥ ।। aniketasaṃstavaparigrahāgrahāḥ svajane jane ca samatāvihāriṇaḥ । tribhavopapattigahanāntadarśino himavadvaneṣu ratim āpnuyuḥ kathaṃ ।।
sukhaduḥkhayor aviṣamapravṛttayo nṛpa yena tena parituṣṭamānasāḥ । satataṃ mṛgā iva nisargatāpasā viharanty anāvṛtavihāragocarāḥ ।। visṛtāṃ bhavadrumaśikhāvalambinīṃ vividhopatāpaparuṣāṃ viṣaktikāṃ । upahātya ye padam upāsate śivaṃ tridive api te narakavāsasaṃjñinaḥ ।।
anubandhiniṃ pratinivārya saṃhatiṃ tamasāṃ kim apy anubhavanti ye sukhaṃ । na sanatkumārabhavane api te ratiṃ viratopasargaratayaḥ prakurvate ।। vanarājayaḥ kusumacitrapādapāḥ girayaḥ kadambatarucumbitāmbudāḥ । saritaś ca haṃsakulabhinnavīcayaḥ paridurbale manasi labdhapravṛttayaḥ ।।
śiraḥkaṃpollasaccārukuṇḍalaḥ sa mahīpatiḥ । sādhu sādhv iti saṃrādhya pratijagrāha tadvacaḥ ।। nyāyoparodhi paripeśalavarṇaśobham akṣūṇakālamadhuraṃ svaparopakāri । vākyaṃ suhṛjjanamukhoccaritaṃ kathaṃ na syād apratigrahavipātitakāntiśobhaṃ ।।
amlāyamānakaruṇārasaśībharāṇi svāntāny anākulapadakramayogikāni । vākyāni sajjanamukhāmburuhacyutāni pradveṣarūkṣam api mānasam ākṣipanti ।। nīceṣv api praṇatinamraśirodharāṇāṃ krūrāśayeṣv api kṛpāmṛdumānasānāṃ । ādyantamadhyamadhurāṇi jinātmajānāṃ vākyāni ko bhuve vimānayituṃ samarthaḥ ।।
prītyutkarṣaparamparām anubhavan kām apy anāyāsinīṃ । svarddhyaivāpratighaṃ vigāhya vighanaṃ khaṃ rājahaṃsā iva ।। sa bhūpatiḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrasaṃkhyā guhā viviktā jalayaṃtraśītāḥ । saṃskārya tebhyaḥ pradadau prasannaḥ pratyekaśo dagdhapunarbhavebhyaḥ ।।
śaratsahasrāṇi saṣaṣṭir eva cakāra teṣāṃ vigatajvarāṇāṃ । pūjāṃ parāṃ dṛṣṭaparāyaṇānāṃ saṃcāriṇām puṇyavanaspatīnāṃ ।। taṃ bodhau sa pariṇamayya puṇyarāśiṃ saṃtyajya prakṛtivināśinaṃ svadehaṃ । trailokyaprathitaparākramaprabhāvo māndhātā kila vasudhādhipo babhūva ।।
saṃkalpānuvidhāyinyas tasyābhūvan vibhūtayaḥ । sarvalokātiśāyinyo nirupāyāsapeśalāḥ ।। puṇyāny evam asau cakāra bhagavān yasmāj jagadbhūtaye tyaktvā rājyavibhūtivistarasukhāny amlāyamānodyamaḥ । tasmāt tatra manaḥ prasādya bhagavaty āścaryaratnākare pātavyaṃ svaparopakāramadhuraṃ tasyaiva vākyāmṛtaṃ ।। iti śrīmeghajātakaṃ catvāriṃśattamaṃ ।।
sahasraśo api saṃtyaktum utsahante svajīvitam । sādhavaḥ sādhumaryādāṃ na muhūrtam api kṣamāḥ ।। tad yathānuśrūyate। bodhisattvabhūtaḥ kilāhaṃ bhagavān aparimlāyamānakaruṇāsaumyadarśano nāgarājo babhūva ।
krodhena tasya saha śāśvatasaṃvirodhaḥ krodhottaraṃ nigaditaṃ samupāgatasya । icchānukūlamadhurā pratisandhilīlā sādhoḥ suyonividhuraiva babhūva tasya ।। saṃprāptakarmavaśitātiśayasya yasya lokā hṛdīva nivasanti kṛpāviśāle । roṣas tataḥ katham uderati śuddhasattvāt padmākarād vikasitād iva citrabhānuḥ ।। kuvalayadalamālākomalaṃ bhogacakraṃ svamaṇikiraṇajālaśrīkarālaṃ sa bibhrat ।
ghanasamaya ivāsīl locanānandabandhuḥ suravarapaticāpodbhāsito vāmbugarbhaḥ ।। atha sa mahāsattvaḥ krodhabahulatāṃ nāgayoner avetya tatpratipakṣakṣamākathām udbhāvayām āsa svaparṣadi ।। na hemamālā maṇidīptiśībharāḥ srajo na citrā makarandapiñjarāḥ । tathābhyalaṃkartum alaṃ śarīriṇāṃ yathā kṣamā sarvaguṇaikaratnakā ।।
manojñarūpā api nāma roṣiṇo viṣādayanty eva manāṃsi dehinām । vimuktakośā iva puṣpapādapāḥ svamūlasaṃsarpibhujaṅgakaṅkaṇāḥ ।। asaṃstutānām api nāma sūratā bhavanti viśrambhaviśeṣabhājanam । iti kṣamāṃ ko na bhajeta buddhimān aśeṣalokāśrayasaṃgrahakṣamām ।। imām avasthāṃ gamitā vidāhināmunā vayaṃ roṣamayena pāpmanā ।
nivṛttavairān api yad viśaṅkate mahājano asmān animittakāhataḥ ।। evam anyathā ca svayūthyān saṃjñāpayām āsa ।। dṛṣṭīviṣānalamucāṃ svamaṇiprabhādbhiḥ pātālarandhragahanāntavisarpiṇībhiḥ । tesāṃ sa pannagavaraḥ śamayāṃ babhūva vāgambubhiś ca hṛdayāni bhujaṅgamānām ।।
sa ca mahātmājanmāntarābhyastapraśamarativihārasādhanaḥ sarvalokottarotkṛṣṭair tair api viṣayair anākalitamānaso viḍambanām iva tām aiśvaryalakṣmīm abhimanyamānaḥ pravivekasukhavihāroparodhinaṃ cādhipatyapariśramam āryanyāyamārgakaṇṭakasthānīyāṃś ca snigdhajanasamāgamān prakṛtidhīramānasaḥ san gṛhe apy araṇyasaṃjñābhāvanāsamarthaḥ saśaṅko gārhasthadoṣam evodbhāvayan svabhavanād abhyudgamya vivikteṣv araṇyāyataneṣu poṣadhaniyamālaṃkṛtaśarīraḥ kālam atināmayām āsa ।। prāyas teṣu praśamavimukho vismayaṃ yāti lokaḥ । nānātaṅkapracayagahane bodhisattvapratijñāḥ ।। atha kadā cit sa mahātmā pratyaraṇyaniviṣṭataruṇatarumaṇḍalaikadeśāvasthito bhujagaviṣopaghātayogyavidyādhareṇa brāhmaṇenopalakṣitaḥ । sa tasya tena niyamaviśeṣaramaṇīyenāśvāsadena tejasvibhāvena vismitamanā nāsmāt pratyavāyo astīti niścitya svajīvikopāyaṃ ca tadgrahaṇasāhasam avetya taṃ bhujagapatiṃ viśrambhamukulitaphaṇacakram āsīnaṃ sahasā mahatā daṇḍena śirasy abhijaghāna taptapāṃsupūgaiś cāsya nayanāni pūrayām āsa mahatyā cainaṃ vararajjvā gāḍhaṃ grīvāyām āmardayāṃ babhūva mūlāgadasaṃmiśreṇa cainaṃ śleṣmaṇā vadanavivareṣu saṃsiktavān vivṛtya cāsya vadanapuṭam ayaḥsaṃdaṃśena daṃṣṭrāḥ samudājahāra ।। lobhaparyākulamānasaś cāsya tīkṣṇena śastreṇa ghanakośopagūḍhamūlāṃ cūḍāmaṇim utpāṭayāṃ cakre pratinakulacalavalayarāśikomale cāsya bhogakuṇḍale bimbopadhāna iva niṣadya viśaśrāma ।।
lajjāmantharakomalālasaphaṇacchattro yayau saṃbhramam । kṣāntyabhyāsavaśāt samīraṇacalattūlāṃśupātopamān ।। khedaṃ nāgavaraḥ sukhocitamayāṃ [?] bheje kriyāṃ cāyatām [?] । tenākāraṇadāruṇena ripuṇā so abhūn nirāstho vaśī ।।
grīṣme prāṇasamāḥ saratnavalayair nāgottamaṃ paspṛśuḥ । lebhe saṃtatavartinīṃ ghanarasāṃ maitrīṃ tadālambanām ।। daṃṣṭrā bisāṅkurasitā vinigūḍhamūlās tasyoccakhāna sa yadā bhujageśvarasya । śalyāpahāriṇi tadā bhiṣajīva tasmin vipre cakāra sa parām upakārisaṃjñām ।।
ārtīyate sma sahajāny api yāni citraṃ sādhuḥ śiromaṇimayāni vibhūṣaṇāni । teṣūddhṛteṣu sa kṛtārthatayā pramodaṃ nikṣiptabhāra iva bhogapatir jagāma ।। gonā । śvāsānilaiḥ sphuṭaviṣāgnikarākarālair ucchoṣayet samakarān api yaḥ samudrān । kṣāntiṃ priyām iva sakhīm upaguhya tasthau svasthas tam eva ca ripuṃ karuṇāyamānaḥ ।। syād bhasmasāc chikharakoṭivipāṭitābhraḥ śailo api dṛṣṭiviṣayaṃ samupetya yasya । pāpātmanā kumudanālam ivoragendro nāsau cukopamṛdito api parānurakṣī ।।
tīvraprakāram upakāram ivāvikāraḥ sehe kṛpāparigataḥ sa yathā yathāryaḥ । krauryāvalepaparuṣaḥ sa tathā tathā taṃ cikleśa pannagavaraṃ vividhair upāyaiḥ ।। karuṇādravam eva durjanaḥ sutarāṃ satpuruṣaṃ prabādhate । mṛdam eva bhinatti kaṇṭakaḥ kaṭhine kuṇṭhaka eva jāyate ।।
sa pīḍyamānaḥ puruṣeṇa tena bhujaṅgarājo vigatavyathena । tam eva rakṣan guṇapakṣasākṣī mumoca na śvāsaviṣaṃ viṣādī ।। yathā yathā pīḍayati sma nāma tam āryakarmāṇam asāv anāryaḥ । tathā tathāsau tadapāyaśaṅkī na cakṣur unmīlayituṃ viṣehe ।।
parāpakārapratipattimārutā durācarās tasya viśuddhakarmaṇaḥ । kṣamāśilādhāraparigrahasthiraṃ na kampayanti sma mano manasvinaḥ ।। ambhojareṇukaṇikā iva saṃpratīcchan nāgottamaḥ kṣitirajo arkakaropataptam । netropaghātapaṭunā paṭunā vimuktaṃ tasmin babhūva sutarāṃ sa parānukampaḥ ।।
nānāpuṣparajo'dhivāsaśucibhiś candraprabhānirmalaiḥ । prītyaivāpacakāra taṃ paribhavaṃ kṣāntyāmbhasevokṣitaḥ ।। evam anyathā cāsau brāhmaṇādhamas taṃ bodhisattvam parikliśya mahati karaṇḍe prakṣipya tena tena paribhraman vārāṇasīṃ nagarīm anuprāptaḥ ।। atha tasya bhujagapates tāṃ rūpasaṃpadam ālokya mahājanaḥ paramavismitamanās taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ mahatyā pūjayā pūjayām āsa ।। atha tasya mahātmanaḥ sumanānāmāntaḥpurāgracarā bhujagayoṣid atītāyām ucitāyāṃ tadāgamanavelāyāṃ taṃ bhogipatim apaśyantī jānānā tasya prakṛtibhadratām anāryakarmārāmatāṃ ca mānuṣahṛdayānāṃ tadatyayāśaṅkinī tīvraśokāyāsavyathitahṛdayā tat tad vikalpya satvaraṃ ruroda ।।
tamasā nirantaravisāriṇaiva me parivaryate nayanagocaraṃ balāt । anirūpitātyayavikalpakātaraṃ dravatīva mānasam idaṃ priyaṃ vinā ।। sphuṭamallikāvanavilāsalāsakā jalayantramandiranirodhaśītalāḥ । sutarāṃ dahanti mama calamārutā dayitapravāsaparitāpinīṃ tanum ।।
pratibhāty apūrvam iva sarvam adya me na ca vedmi kāham iti tena varjitā । vyasane sa eva śaraṇaṃ mama priyo virahe tu tasya maraṇaṃ parāyaṇam ।। maṇivedikākiraṇapāṭalormayo gṛhadīrghikā na ramayanti me manaḥ । priyavipravāsaparitāpaviplutaṃ sphuṭapadmakośamakarandavāsitāḥ ।।
diśatūttamāni jagaduttamadyutir mama maṅgalāni bhagavān sa eva tu । na bhavāntare api viraho yathā bhaved dayitena tena niravadyakarmaṇā ।। virahānubandhavirasāḥ samāgamā jagato araparvapariṇāminī sthitiḥ । iti yaj jagāda manaso ativallabhaḥ samupasthitaṃ tad idam adya vaiśasam ।।
vikasatsphuliṅgam anilākulārciṣaṃ dahanaṃ viśāmi bahuduḥkhabhāginī । tanum utsṛjāmi śikharād girer imām avaśiṣyate kim aparaṃ mamāyuṣaḥ ।। yadi so adya naiti sukhasaumyadarśano mama mūrtimān avikalo manorathaḥ । svayam eva dhakṣyati mamedam āśrayaṃ hṛdayajvalas tumulaśokadāruṇaḥ ।। iti sā rurāva kurarīva viklavā nayanāmbudurdinamukhī tapasvinī ।
vasudhātale galitahāramekhalā bhujagāṅganā pativiyogaśaṅkinī ।। atha sumanā nāma yoṣid bodhisattvam anveṣamānā vārāṇasīṃ nagarīm anuprāptā dadarśa cainaṃ mahāsattvaṃ paramadāruṇām avasthām upagataṃ dṛṣṭvā ca tīvraśokāyāsavyathitahṛdayā provāca । kva dayita gatās tās tā daṃṣṭrā bisāṅkuradhūsarāḥ । vigalitahṛdayā krūreṇaitat kṛpātmaka kena te ।।
tejaḥ kopaviṣātisaṅgarabhasaṃ kiṃ proṣitaṃ bhoginām । yena tvaṃ vyasanaṃ duruttaram idaṃ prāpto vināśāya te ।। krauryaṃ tvayy api nāma sādhucarite pāpātmanāṃ jāyate । nāthānātha ivāpadaṃ katham imāṃ prāptas tvam āyāsinīm ।।
bodhisattvas tu pratyagrakopaśokakaluṣitādhyāśayātmanām avetya tūṣṇīm eva babhūva ।। sā punar abravīt ।। kasyāpriyaṃ jīvitam ādyajātaṃ kālena kelīṃ saha kaḥ karoti । tvadapriyāriṣṭaniviṣṭaceṣṭo lokāntaraṃ ko abhyanugantukāmaḥ ।। śītābhilāṣī pravivikṣur agniṃ ko mārutoddhataśikhākalāpam । āditsate krūraviṣaṃ bhujaṅgaṃ kaḥ puṣpadāmākṛtivipralabdhaḥ ।।
udadhiparikhām adyaivaināṃ dahāmi vasundharāṃ sanaganagaragrāmārāmāṃ svadṛṣṭihutāśanaiḥ । na mama hṛdayaṃ śāntiṃ yāti tvadapriyatāḍitaṃ dahati yadi na krodhāgnir māṃ purā niravagrahaḥ ।। atha bodhisattvas tāṃ tapasvinīm aviṣahyakopāgnipradīptamānasāṃ hlādayann iva tadāmṛtaśiśirābhir vāgbhir ity abravīt ।। alam alaṃ mā gā bhadre vai kopasya cetovidāhinaḥ । prakṛtiduḥkheṣu ko bhūyaḥ sattveṣu duḥkhāni cintayet ।।
duḥkhahetau vartamāneṣu śocyeṣu saṃkleśabhāgiṣu kaḥ parākramet ।। duḥkhāya svahitakramārteṣu dehiṣu na mama daṃṣṭrotpāṭanād duḥkhaṃ na ca daṇḍasaṃpātajā rujāḥ ।। duḥkhayanti mānasaṃ caṇḍi tvadvākkarkaśās tudanti mām ।। bodhisaṃprāptaye cittaṃ yadaivotpāditaṃ purā । vayaṃ tadaiva lokānām ādheyakriyatāṃ gatāḥ ।। kopavahnimlāyamānā punaḥ saiva tvam anyeva lakṣyase ।।
candralekheva cāmbare vikasadghanadhūmasaṃbādhadhūsare ।। kiṃ ca ।। karmāparādhajanitaṃ yadi duḥkham etat kopāvakāśa iha ko nu mama dvijātau । karmendhanoddhataśikhāśakalākulebhyaḥ kupyet kathaṃ na matimān narakānalebhyaḥ ।।
tad alaṃ kopadainyena tava cetovidāhinā । svagṛhān eva gacchasva saṃtyāgaṃ ca kuruṣva me ।। sā bhartur abhiprāyaṃ saṃpādayantī tadvacanāpyāyitahṛdayā vigatakopasaṃrambhā babhūva ।। kopoparāgavigame vivṛto adhimātraḥ snehaḥ priye viṣamavartini nāgavadhvā ।
udghāṭitābhrapaṭalasphuṭadigvibhāge khe niḥsapatna iva candramasaḥ prakāśaḥ ।। śokāśrunayanapariplutā ceti bodhisattvam abravīt ।। kuto me duḥkhabhāginyā gehaṃ ārya tvayā vinā । ihaiva śoṣam eṣyāmi yā gatis tava sā mama ।।
viṣamasthaṃ parityajya tvām anātha sukhaidhitam । kānta kena sukhenāhaṃ drakṣyāmi svajanaṃ punaḥ ।। sukhe samānatāṃ gatvā duḥkhe jahyāṃ yadi priyam । anāryām akṛtajñāṃ māṃ dhārayiṣyati bhūḥ katham ।।
pratibhāti jagac chūnyaṃ tvayā virahitaṃ mama । tvaṃ me jīvitasarvasvaṃ tvaṃ bandhus tvaṃ parāyaṇam ।। bodhisattvo atha tāṃ sādhvīṃ bahalasnehaviklavām । anukampāvaśāt sādhur īdṛśaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।।
adṛṣṭapūrvavyasanā sukhasaṃvardhitā priye । parikleśam imaṃ soḍhum akṣamā tvam anindite ।। mayi sneho asti yadi te duḥkhaṃ me yadi necchasi । adṛṣṭam adya māṃ kṛtvā tad gaccha tvaṃ svam ālayam ।।
atha sā tair bodhisattvavaco'dbhir ākleditahṛdayā duḥkhadaurmanasyaparyākulamānasā niśīthe kāśikārājam upetya karuṇākulatarākṣareṇa vacasā kṛtāñjalir avocat ।। āpadgatānāṃ vyasanakṣayāya tvaṃ pañcamaḥ pārthiva lokapālaḥ । trāyasva mām āpadi vartamānāṃ dīnām anāthāṃ jagadekanātha ।। atha sa rājā tad atibhāsuraṃ vapur avalokya kim idaṃ kathaṃ cety utpannajātasaṃbhramaḥ sādaram utthāya paryaṅkapṛṣṭhāt tāṃ nāgayoṣitam etad avocat ।।
vyāhārasphuṭacitravarṇakaraṇo divyaprabhāvaś ca te । mālāṃ phulladalām ivādya śirasā samyak pratīcchāmy aham ।। athāsau bhujagavadhūs tena tasya rājño abhijātyapeśalena vacasā samānanditamanasā provāca ।। āśāvaśānāṃ naradeva ko anyo manorathaṃ pūrayituṃ samarthaḥ ।
tyaktvā bhavantaṃ jagato hitāya prajāpater vaṃśam ivāvatīrṇam ।। nāgāṅganāṃ mām avagaccha rājaṃs tvaddeśaparyantakṛtādhivāsām । āpadgataṃ mānada pannagendraṃ trāyasva kṛtyaṃ mama tad garīyaḥ ।। rājovāca ।। bhagini kas tavāsau bhujagavaraḥ ।। sā provāca ।। bhartā mama prāṇadhaneśvaro asau nyāyopradeṣṭā ca gurur garīyān ।
piteva nityaṃ hitasaṃvidhātāsukhe ca viśrambhaniratyayaś ca ।। atha sa bhūpatis tena tasyāḥ svāmyanurāgaśībhareṇa caritenābhiprasāditaḥ ।। premodbhāvitam āpadi sthirataraṃ prodghāṭitā bhadratā । loke sādhupativratatvam iti te khyātiḥ sthitā śāśvatī ।।
tyaktvā priyaṃ jīvitam apy ato ahaṃ puṇyaprabhāvopanataṃ ca rājyam । saṃpūrayiṣyāmi manorathaṃ te paśyādya bhadre dayitaṃ vimuktam ।। atha sa rājā tasya brāhmaṇasyāntikāt taṃ nāgarājānaṃ mahatā mūlyena niṣkrīya parameṇa sapatnīkaṃ svabhavanaṃ praveśya mahārhasiṃhāsanopaviṣṭam abhyarcayām āsa ।। atha bodhisattvas tena tasya rājño atyadbhutena niṣkāraṇopakārasaṃbhrameṇākṛṣṭamanāḥ provācainam ।। asaṃstute nāma tavāyam ādaro mayi prasādasthirabhaktipeśalaḥ ।
kṛtopakāreṣv api yo na dṛśyate pṛthagjaneṣu sukhānubuddhiṣu ।। prakāśiteyaṃ guṇapakṣapātitā prajānurāgo bahulīkṛtas tvayā । guṇe vivardhasva tad uttarottarair guṇeṣu bhadraṃ jagatāṃ avasthitam ।। iti saṃrādhya rājānaṃ tam asau bhujageśvaraḥ ।
anubaddho dayitayā kṛpayeva gṛhān yayau ।। iti śrīnāgajātakaṃ catvāriṃśattamam ।। athāśoko mahārāja upaguptaṃ yatiṃ gurum । kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayac ca tathādarāt ।।
bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitam । tad yathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me arhati ।। iti tena narendreṇa prārthite sa jinātmajaḥ । upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat ।।
śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditam । tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā caivaṃ śubhe cara ।। nāsti vipākaparyanta upakārāpakārayoḥ । saṃbuddhe sadgurau tasmāt kartavyam upakārakam ।।
tad yathāstāṃ mahāsattvau saṃbuddhopāsakau purā । kadā cit tāv ubhau grāmaṃ gacchantau saṃgatau pathi ।। saṃbuddhapratimāṃ tatra puṇyarāśim ivottamām । tāṃ samīkṣya tayor ekaḥ praṇatvaivaṃ tam abravīt ।।
aho bata mahāpuṇyarāśir ayaṃ virājate । bhāgyena dṛśyate asmābhir adya mitra praṇamyatām ।। iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvāparas tam abravīt । aho bata mahān mitra pāparāśir ayaṃ nv iti ।।
iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā prathamaḥ sa upāsakaḥ । karṇau pidhāya hastābhyāṃ tam evaṃ paryabhāṣata ।। dhik tvām asadbuddhim asatpralāpinam [!] evaṃ hy api tvaṃ pratibhāṣase atra । kasmān muneḥ śāstur upāsako api saddharmamūrtiṃ pratinindase adya ।।
kathaṃ na jihvā patitā tavānanād asatpralāpāpahatā tapasvinī । apuṇyarāśir bhagavān iti bruvan kathaṃ na magnas tvam are rasātale ।। dhig apraśastām asatāṃ duratyayāṃ pṛthagjanānāṃ prakṛtiṃ calācalām । vimarśam aprāpya yatheṣṭacāriṇī karoti yā lokam apāyagocaram ।।
sudāruṇair āyudhabhīmadarśanair arātibhiḥ sārdham aho varaṃ gatam । tvayā suhṛcchadmanigūḍhapāpmanā padaṃ na caikaṃ vitathapralāpinā ।। namanti yaṃ brahmavido maharṣayaḥ punāti yo viśvam idaṃ vṛṣāṃśubhiḥ । apuṇyarāśir yadi sa vratīśvaras tathāgataḥ puṇyanidhiḥ kuto aparaḥ ।।
muneḥ paroddhāranimittamātram apy upaiti yasyoddhṛtakalmaṣo api san । sa yogaparyantavidāṃ dhuri sthito na puṇyarāśir yadi ko nv ihāparaḥ ।। na yasya buddhiḥ pratihanyate kva cin na ca praheyāvayavo avaśiṣyate । na cāsti saṅgo jagadarthasādhane sa puṇyarāśir na kathaṃkathāntaśaḥ ।।
taduktaṃ sa samākarṇya dvitīyopāsakas [!] tataḥ । prāgalbhavacasā bhūya āyuṣmantaṃ tam abravīt ।। hitakāmyatayā niratyayaṃ vacanaṃ kāmam idaṃ sakhe tava । anuyujya tathāpi śobhate vitathaṃ sādhur udīrayan bhavān ।।
mama bhaktir udāraśāsane sugate yā paramānukampake । viditā tava sā tathāpi māṃ sahasā saumya kathaṃ vigarhase ।। sāyāsaṃ sabhayaṃ prasaṅgavirasaṃ dhig laukikaṃ saṃgatam । gacchaty ekapade kṣayaṃ paricayaṃ vikṣipya mūrdhno antikam ।।
etat tenoditaṃ śrutvā prathamaḥ sa upāsakaḥ । anyathā tadvaco matvā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat ।। aho hy anyad anenoktam anyan mayā vikalpitam । iti cintāviṣaṇṇātmā tasthau lajjāhatāśayaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā sa ca sahāyas taṃ lajjāvanamitānanam । tadabhiprāyam ājñātuṃ prasahya caivam abravīt ।। sādho kiṃ manyase hy atra yat te lajjāhataṃ mukham । tāvat te yad abhiprāyaṃ tat pracakṣva mamāgrataḥ ।।
tasyaitad vacanaṃ śrutvā sa āyuṣmān upāsakaḥ । tanmano'ntargataṃ sarvam abhiprāyaṃ vyamuñcata ।। śrīsaubhāgyaprakarṣaṃ bhavagatiṣu paraṃ prāpya nirdvandvaramyam । jñātvā prāpnoti śāntaṃ katham iva na mahān puṇyarāśir bhavet saḥ ।।
dattvā palālaśakalasrajam agrasattve lebhe bhavopaśamaśāntisukhāni nārī । yasminn acintyacaritātiśayaprabhāve kiṃ puṇyarāśir ayam ity avidagdham etat ।। kośātakīkusumam api pradāya stūpe muneḥ paramakāruṇikasya yasya । bhuktvālaye guṇavibhūtisukhaprakarṣaṃ lebhe aṅganāmṛtapurapratipatsamṛddhim ।।
sphītāṃ martyendralakṣmīm anavanatasitacchattrahāsābhirāmām । lebhe paścān narendraḥ katham iva sa na bhoḥ puṇyarāśir maharṣiḥ ।। prasahya paṅkāṅkam ṛṣer varāhaḥ [!] caitye vapur yasya ciraṃ sa eva । tasyaiva dharmasya sudharmatāsau yadādhipatyena bhavād vimuktaḥ ।।
kiyān prasādo jaḍacetanānāṃ sakhe tiraścāṃ guṇaniścayo vā । kṣetrasya tasyaiva tu sā vibhūtir yenātra sattvāḥ saphalī bhavanti ।। vyāmābhāpariveṣiṇīṃ bhagavato buddhasya mūrtiṃ purā । taddhetoś ca śamaṃ jagāma sa śikhī dhārāmbusikto yathā ।।
buddhānāṃ tad udīkṣyatāṃ bhagavatāṃ saṃmohanidrācchidām । prāg evābhimukhāśayasya viduṣaḥ śāstur guṇāmbhonidheḥ ।। sarvākāraparopakāramadhuraṃ pūrvābhisaṃskārajam । sthānaṃ sarvabhavopasargavigamād ekāntaśāntaṃ śivam ।।
saṃpṛktāsyapuṭo mamāra sugate cetaḥ prasādya kṣaṇam । janmāmbhonidhim uttatāra vipulaṃ niḥsṛtya mārge plavam ।। apāyapātālatalāvalambī suro munīndraṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadya । svapuṇyasopānaparamparābhiḥ samārurohāgryataraṃ vimānam ।।
nāmnaivānupamasya puṇyamahatīm ālokya nāndīṃ pumān । chāntiṃ kām api vāgatītaviṣayāṃ prahlādasaṃvardhanīm ।। tam anupamaviśeṣācintyacaryārahasyam । padam amaram ahāryaṃ puṇyarāśiṃ vadāmi ।।
iti tadgaditaṃ śrutvā sa itara upāsakaḥ । tam āyuṣmantam ālokya punar evaṃ samabravīt ।। samyag abhihitaṃ sādho bhavatātra tathāpi ca । mamāpy evam abhiprāyaṃ śrūyatāṃ sāṃprataṃ sakhe ।।
yatrāvicchinnamaitrījalakalaśaśatakṣālitāntaḥprakope । gāhante avīcim ajñāḥ katham iva sa jino apuṇyarāśir na tuṅgaḥ ।। pārthagjanyaviṣasya vṛttim aśivām udbhāvayan karmaṇā । nāgendraḥ pṛthubhīmabhogapaṭalo nādyāpi nirmucyate ।।
yat sarvāyatanopatāpavirasām ākarṣati prāṇinām । prāptaḥ śāntim apuṇyarāśir asatāṃ tasmāt sa sattvottamaḥ ।। kīṭaḥ kopopadagdho nṛparathacaraṇāghātavicchinnamūrdhā । śvabhraṃ tasmād viveśa pratihatatimiro apuṇyarāśis tato asau ।।
prāptābhijñe mṛdur api kṛtaś cetanāsaṃniveśaḥ । saḥ sarttā [?] bhavasukhalavāsvādalagnābhilāṣam ।। lokair duḥkhair viṣayakṛpaṇair indriyair vipralabdham । mātuṃ teṣu prabhavati pumān ko apakāropakārau ।।
visphoṭasphuṭitārdramāṃsaguḍako bībhatsasarvāśrayaḥ । tat ko nāma na pūjayet sahṛdayaḥ puṇyārṇavaṃ jaṅgamam ।। tasmāt praduṣṭamanasāṃ bhagavān apuṇyarāśiḥ prasannamanasāṃ tu sa puṇyarāśiḥ । paryāyato vigatasarvasavāsanāntaḥsaṃkleśakilbiṣadaśo viṣayāntadarśī ।।
prakṛīḍantī karakisalayapracyutena pramādāt । kiṃ saṃprāptā na kanakavatī bāhuvicchedaduḥkam ।। nṝṇāṃ dhvāntam apākaroty aviralaṃ rūpopalabdhyai karaiḥ । buddho apy evam apuṇyapuṇyanicayaḥ sāmānyanātho api san ।।
iti tāv upāsakau buddhaguṇamāhātmyakīrtanam । kṛtvā parasparaṃ sattvaṃ pavitrīkṛtya jagmatuḥ ।। evaṃ matvā mahārāja saṃbuddhe sadgurau mudā । śraddhayā satkṛtiḥ kāryā nāpakṛtiḥ kathaṃ cana ।।
śāstary avajñāmalināśayānāṃ bhūmir vidāraṃ na dadāti sadyaḥ । buddhaprasādadravacetasāṃ vā na jāyate ratnamayī vicitraṃ ।। ko apy eṣa karmāntarasaṃnirodhaḥ puṇyaprabhāvātiśayo vicitraḥ । karmāṇi yat pātraviśeṣajāni sadyo na nṝṇāṃ phalam udvamanti ।।
tasyaiva kāpīyam ṛṣer acintyā vibhūtir āveṇikayogasādhvī । yenātra kṛtvāpi manaḥpradoṣaṃ sadyo na pātālatalaṃ viśanti ।। kāryā bhaktir bhagavati jine nirjitāntaḥsapatne । yāvan nedaṃ bhavati bhuvanaṃ buddhakāntāraghoram ।।
sarvākārāparatavitathagrāhanidrāprasaṅgāḥ । yatrotpādo bhavati bhuvanasvāmināṃ bhūtabhūtyai ।। yāvat saṃbuddhabhānoḥ pravacanakiraṇā lokam udbhāvayanti । loke durdṛṣṭimeghā vipadaśanimukhā durnivārāḥ sphuranti ।।
evaṃ me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā te kathyate mayā । tad evaṃ hi parijñāya kartavyaṃ bhajanaṃ muneḥ ।। ye bhajanti sadā buddhaṃ na te gacchanti durgatim । niḥkleśāḥ sabalān mārāñ jitvā yānti jinālayam ।।
ye ca śṛṇvanti saddharmaṃ te api na yānti durgatim । sarvadā satsukhaṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīm ।। ye arcayanti mudā saṃghān na te api yānti durgatim । sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayānti śubhālaye ।।
evaṃ matvā mahārāja triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ । sarvasattvahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃvṛtiṃ saṃpracāraya ।। tena te sarvadā bhadram ihāmutrāpi saṃbhavet । kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtiṃ vā samāpnuyāḥ ।।
iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatir mudā । tatheti saṃpratijñāya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ ।। puṇyarāśyavadānaṃ tad idaṃ ye śraddhayā mudā । śrāvayanty anumodante śṛṇvanti ca samāhitāḥ ।।
sarve api te mahāsattvāḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ । saddharmaguṇasaukhyāni bhuktvā yānti jinālayam ।। ।। iti puṇyarāśyavadānaṃ samāptam ।। mūlaṃ malānāṃ pravadanti jātiṃ jātiprapañcopaśamapravīṇāḥ । tathāgatāś cāvitathapratijñāḥ saṃbhodhisattvāś ca viśuddhasattvāḥ ।।
tadyathānuśrūyate । bodhisattvaḥ kila lokābhimataguṇābhilakṣite mahati brāhmaṇakule janma pratijagrāha । kiraṇair iva śuklapakṣacandraḥ svaguṇair eva sahābhivardhamānaḥ । paramāṃ svakulasya cihnaśobhāṃ prathimānaṃ gamayāṃ babhūva sādhuḥ ।।
vayasi prathame api vartamāno viṣayeṣv atibaddhamānaso asau । atimānuṣaceṣṭitasvabhāvo jagatāṃ smayabhājanaṃ babhūva ।। so aparyavasitakukāryaparyākulam upaśamavirodhiprakṛṣṭopāyāsam arthopārjanapradhānakāmarativyavahārāsārakarmadharmabhūyiṣṭham avinayakalahavairavigrahāyatanam īrṣyāmātsaryacauryādiniketabhūtaṃ śokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsabahulaṃ māyāśāṭhyamadamānagahanaṃ sāhasāvalepādhiṣṭhitam anāryavyavahārānupravṛttijihmasattvabhāvaṃ pramādapadasthānam anekarūpaparibhavopasṛṣṭaṃ saṃnihitadainyam anabhibhūtaviṣādaṃ pratyāsannavighātabhayadaurgatyam aviṣahyopadravasamudraṃ kaṇṭakagarbhādabhraśvabhrapratibhayākaram apāsya gārhasthyam anyatamam aśramapadam abhyalaṃcakāra । bahucchalaṃ so atha bahuvyalīkaṃ bahūpasargaṃ bahudoṣaduṣṭam ।
apāsya gārhasthyam anarthamūlaṃ tapovanaṃ śāntam alaṃcakāra ।। sarobhir unnidrapalāśakoṣakuśeśayendīvaracitratoyaiḥ । alaṃkṛtaṃ bālakaśerunīlapratīrasaṃsuptaśarārihaṃsaiḥ ।। mīnāvalīraśanayā saritopagūḍhaṃ snehād iva praṇayinaṃ priyayā prakāmam ।
sarvartupuṣpaphaladaiḥ svajanair ivāntar bālapravālaharitais tarubhir niruddham ।। vyālais tapasvibhir ivākṛtimātrarūkṣaiḥ paryākulam jalatṛṇāṅkuratuṣṭacittaiḥ । taṃ kānanāntam upagamya sa bodhisattvo dharmo avatīrṇa iva vigrahavān vyarājat ।। gṛhasthabhāve ape sa vartamāno janmāntarābhyastavivekavāsaḥ ।
āgāradoṣair aparikṣatātmā viśeṣayām āsa tapovanasthān ।। pramādināṃ kāpuruṣāśrayāṇām । utkaṇṭhayanti pravivekayogyās ta eva śāntāḥ satataṃ vanāntāḥ ।। abhyastanaiṣkramyasukhotsavānāṃ satāṃ pravāsā iva gehavāsāḥ ।
mṛgāṅganākuñcitapallavāni vanāni teṣāṃ bhavanottamāni ।। parigraheṣv eva vighātabuddhiḥ saṃtoṣa eva svadhanānurāgaḥ । yeṣāṃ gṛhe cārakavāsasaṃjñā teṣāṃ na citro vanasaṃnivāsaḥ ।। tasya pūrvajanmaparamparābhyāsavāsanāghanasnehagauravaniratyayāś catvāraḥ sahāyā babhūvuḥ vāyasaḥ pārāvato bhujago mṛgaś ca । te tadājñāsaṃpādanaikatānamanasaḥ svayonividhinā dharmakriyāsauṣṭhavena jagaty abhilakṣitā babhūvuḥ ।
chandopaghātavihateṣv aparāyaṇeṣu tiryakṣu mohabahuleṣv adhikaṃ vihbānti । dharmānurāgaviśadāḥ pratipattiśobhās tāmisrapakṣarajanīṣv iva dīpamālāḥ ।। vismāpayanti sutarāṃ viguṇāśrayiṇyo dharmakriyāḥ karaṇapāṭavayogaramyāḥ । grīṣmoṣmadurgamatarāsu vanasthalīṣu prodbhidyamānakamalā iva paṅkajinyaḥ ।।
teṣām ekadā snehaniryantraṇaramaṇīyāvasthānapravṛttasaṃkathānām ayaṃ viniścayo babhūva । kiṃ nu khalu bhavanto atiśayena duḥkhaṃ manyante । teṣāṃ dakṣatām ivodbhāvayan prathamataraṃ vāyasaḥ provāca । nehāsti kṣudho anyat paramaṃ duḥkham । kutaḥ na vyādhayo na ca jarā na suḥrdviyogo nāniṣṭasaṃgamamayā vyasanaprakārāḥ । duḥkhāni tāny upaharanti janasya yāni hrī vipravāsaparitāpakarī jighatsoḥ ।। duruttarakṣārataraṅgamālinīm upāgatā vaitaraṇīṃ pramādinaḥ ।
bubhukṣayā yan nigiranty ayoguḍān tato asti na kṣutsadṛśo aparaḥ kaliḥ ।। kaḍevarāvaskaranirjharasravanmalopalepākamanīyadarśanaḥ । rujā parīto api pipāsati stanaṃ yad arbhakaḥ kṣudvyasanaṃ tato mahat ।। vinākṛtaḥ prāṇasamair api priyair gato api śokasya vaśaṃ vidāhinaḥ ।
yad aśrumiśrān kavaḍān niṣevate tato bhayaṃ kṣut paramaṃ jino abravīt ।। jātaḥ kule mahati mānamadāvalipte kṣudvikṣato abhyudayakāla iva praharṣāt । uccheṣapiṇḍam api nāma nṛpasya bhuṅkte yat sārameya iva kaṣṭataraṃ kim anyat ।। pratyantavāsaratayas tṛṇamātratuṣṭā yat tāpasā iva paravyasanānabhijñāḥ ।
lakṣyībhavanti hariṇāḥ paritaḥ śarāṇāṃ kṣudduḥkham atra niyamena paraimi hetum ।। marmacchidāpi pavanena viśasyamānā hikkāsphuradgalakakaṇṭhavikāradehāḥ । āhārayanti picunāpi yad annaleśān na kṣutsamaṃ vyasanam asti tataḥ prajānām ।। sattvāḥ prāthamakalpikāḥ svakiraṇajvālāvalīmālinaḥ । yat pretā iva vartayanti kṛpaṇāḥ kṛcchropalabdhāśanāḥ ।।
klinnāni krimisaṃkulāni vighṛṇāḥ khādanty amedhyāni ca । anye asthīni cirojjhitāny adhṛtayaḥ kṣudvikṣatā bhuñjate ।। kṣudduḥkhopanipātavismṛtabhayā hṛtvāmiṣaṃ bhuñjate । śūlāmāṃsalavābhilāṣakṛpaṇā gacchanti ke cit kṣayam ।।
vividhāny api bhojanāni bhuktvā bhavane sve maṇihemabhājaneṣu । śitakaṇṭakavikṣatāgrahastā bubhuje sā badarāṇi satyabhāmā ।। śāpotsargānugrahān mlānaśaktir dikparyantakhyātakīrtiprakāśaḥ । viśvāmitro yac cakhāda śvamāṃsaṃ kṣudduḥkhānāṃ tena datto niyogaḥ ।। bālaḥ putraḥ premasarvasvabhūto yat kāntāre khādito dampatibhyām ।
kṣudduḥkhebhyo nāsti duḥkhaṃ tato anyaj janmāṭavyāṃ dhāvatāṃ krūrarūpam ।। yācñādainyān mlānavaktraprasādā dehīty evaṃ vyāharanty apragalbham । dvāri sthitvā vidviṣāṃ kṣudvilolāḥ kiṃ manyadhve duḥkham asmād balīyaḥ ।। athaiṣāṃ pārāvataḥ provāca । satyaṃ balavat kṣudduḥkham । api tu mamābhiprāyaḥ śrūyatām ।
rāga eva mahad duḥkham iti me niścitā matiḥ । kṣut kariṣyati kiṃ yasmād bhasmanāpi nivāryate ।। vāyvambujīrṇataruparṇabhujo api nāma dīrghopavāsaparikarśitagātrayantrāḥ । andhībhavanti munayaḥ skhalitaprabhāvā rāgena duḥpratividhānasamudbhavena ।।
amlānacandrakiraṇāsv api yāminīṣu protphālitābhravivareṣv api vā dineṣu । andho adhamo bhavati rāgaparājitātmā tasmān na rāgasadṛśaḥ kalir asti loke ।। lajjāṃ nimīlayati sarvaguṇāgrabhūtāṃ kīrtiṃ kalaṅkayati nirvikalaprasādām । dharmātmanām api ca nāma tiraskaroti śreyāṃsi meruśikharapratimāni rāgaḥ ।।
nāyaṃ vayas tulayati pragataṃ narāṇāṃ nāpekṣate kulaviśuddhimayīṃ vyavasthām । lokāpavādagahanāny api laṅghayitvā saṃkalparāgaturagaḥ svamatena yāti ।। saṃmūrchitaḥ kusumahāsiṣu mallikānāṃ gulmeṣu vārikaṇakaṇṭakito nabhasvān । saṃtāpayaty anupaśāntavikalparāgaṃ ceto narasya sutarām aparīkṣakasya ।।
sūkṣmāṇi saṃdhigahanāny api cāvagāhya svapratyayā bahuvidhāni matāntarāṇi । medhāvino api nanu rāgapiśācavaśyāḥ saṃprāpnuvanti paramaṃ smṛtivipralopam ।। hatvāpi rāgaviṣabījavijṛṃbhitāni svabhyastayogapadavīsthirabuddhayo api । yoṣinmukhāny alakapallavitāny udīkṣya bhraṣṭā bhavanti tapasaḥ paśubhiḥ samānāḥ ।।
dṛṅmārgaheyam avahatya balaṃ malānām ekāvaśiṣṭabhavabandhanatantavo api । āryā manaḥsthitibhidānugatāḥ smareṇa lajjālavo apy anubhavanti daśām anāryām ।। uccaiḥ śiro vahati tāvad ayaṃ prajāsu yāvan na kāmakalidurlalitāny upāste । āliṅgitaś ca puruṣo madanajvareṇa śvā saṃkaṭasthita iva prakhalīkṛtaś ca ।।
kaṇṭhopāntavirodhagadgadataraṃ kūjañ chanaiḥ pṛṣṭhato rāgād raktatarekṣaṇaḥ sacakitaṃ nirbhartsyamāno muhuḥ । śyenāyātam asaṃpradhārya dayitām anveti pārāvato rāgābhyāsakalaṅkitasya manasaḥ kā vañcanā dūrataḥ ।। mānātyunnatamānasāś ca sakalaṃ paśyanty adhastāj jagat । ājñā mūrdhabhir udvahanti kṛpaṇā mālām ivāmlāyinīm ।। jitvārātīn samaravijayakhyātaśauryāvalepān āyāminyo jagati vitatāḥ kīrtayo yaiḥ samantāt । bhinnās te api prakṛticapalair aṅganāvākyabāṇair nirmaryādāḥ punar ayaśasā jīvalokaṃ sphuranti ।।
bhavati sahasā yāsāṃ trāso gṛheṣu savepathuḥ । bahalatimiracchannān deśāñ chivārutabhīṣaṇān ।। khidyante saṃcarantyaḥ priyavidhṛtakarāmbhoruhā yās taruṇyaḥ । mārgān prāvṛḍniśāsu drutapadarabhasaṃ tā vyatikramya yānti ।।
vepante navavāricūrṇaśiśiraiḥ spṛṣṭāḥ kadambānilair bālā jālagavākṣapakṣavisṛtair yā ramyaharmyāśritāḥ । dhārāpātaviśīrṇapuṣparacanāḥ sāraṅgaparyākulās tā paṅkāṅkitamūkanūpuraravā rātrau vrajanty adhvanā ।। jvālāś cāgner gataghanaśaraccandrikāśleṣaśītāḥ । sāmyaṃ yānti bhramaravirutair dāmabhir mālatīnām ।। sarvāyatanonmāthī tasmād rāgo mahad duḥkham ity ukte bhujago abravīt । nanu khalu duḥkham rāgaś cittaviparyāsakṛd durācāraḥ । krodhaṃ tu duḥkhataram ity avaimi cetojvalaṃ tu mūlam । kutaḥ
vīṇāveṇuravānubaddhamadhurastrīgitaramye gṛhe । krodhād duḥkhataraṃ na duḥkham aparaṃ kiṃ cit tato vidyate ।। viśrambhāyatanatvam abhyupagataiḥ prāyas tiraścām api । yan mohād ṛṣibhir na duḥkham aparaṃ krodhāt tato vidyate ।।
bālaiś ca stanacūcukārpitamukhaiḥ sāvegam unnāditam । rudro yat tripuram dadāha vighṛṇaḥ krodhasya tad vaikṛtam ।। strīṇāṃ bāṣpakaṇāḥ karālataralā no pakṣmalā dṛṣṭayaḥ । rājñāṃ krodhaviṣāśivasya manasaḥ kiṃ nāma duḥkhaṃ tataḥ ।।
garbhādhāraṇayantraṇām avigaṇayyāpāyikāṃ mātaraṃ satkārātiśayakṣamaṃ ca pitaraṃ snehadravādhyāśayam । yad viśrambhaniratyayāṃś ca suhṛdo ghnanti kṣatādhyāśayāḥ krodhasyaiva vipākadāruṇatarās tā vṛttayaḥ sādhavaḥ ।। duḥśodhānām avikalamalālīḍhagūḍhāśayānām । krodhāviṣṭā vacanaviśikhaiḥ saṃmukhaṃ ghnanty anāryāḥ ।। jvālācakrakrakacakalilān krodhano yāty apāyān ।
śrīvidveṣo na ripur aparaḥ krodhatulyo asti yasmāt ।। yasmin rakto bhavati puruṣas tatra kuryāt priyāṇi dviṣṭo yasmai tadadhikatarāṇy apriyāṇy eva dhatte । alpāvadye avigatarajasā tena roṣaḥ praviṣṭaḥ krodhaṃ krodhopaśamakuśalā vadyayoniṃ vadanti ।। saṃrambhāpahṛtottarīyavasanāṃ vicchinnakaṇṭheguṇām । sphīte yat sadasi prakāmacapalāḥ krodhasya tā vipluṣaḥ ।।
lokānām animittapeśalarasaḥ snehārthakārī suhṛt । rājñā durjanavallabhasya nikaṣaṃ krodhasya tat prāhṛtam ।। anekādīnavamayo vinipātī manojvalaḥ । ity evaṃ sarvaduḥkhānāṃ krodhārir dhuri vartate ।।
mṛgo abravīt । samyag vaktum etad bhujagapate krodhavaiśasaṃ tīvram । maraṇabhayād adhikataraṃ duḥkham ahaṃ nāvagacchāmi । kutaḥ maraṇopanipātakātarāṇāṃ kamanīyāny api mārabandhanāni । na mano ramayanti yaj janānāṃ na duḥkham ataḥ paraṃ paraimi ।। suhṛdāṃ vadanāni vīkṣamāṇo ghanabāṣpāmbutaraṅgadurdināni । labhate vyasanaṃ yad antakāle na tato duḥkham avaimi kaṣṭam anyat ।।
pavanair avidheyaduḥkhaśīlaiḥ karapatrair iva pāṭyamānadehāḥ । paralokamahāprapātaśaṅkāḥ kṛpaṇā duḥkham avāpnuvanti tīvram ।। paripāṇḍukapolamaṇḍalāni śvasanamlānavipāṭalādharāṇi । dayitāvadanāni nānukampāṃ janayanty antakadantavikṣatānām ।।
jananī malapaṅkadigdhaveṇī sutaviśrambhaniratyayopacārā । upamṛtyum udīkṣya śokapaṅke vinimajjaty aparāyaṇā rudantī ।। calatāṃ tṛṇaparṇapallavānāṃ dhvanim ākarṇya vane mṛgā vasantaḥ । anapekṣya parasparaṃ dravāmaḥ svasutān apy avadhūya mṛtyubhītāḥ ।।
kaṭhinopalaśarkarākarāleṣv analapluṣṭatṛṇācaladrumeṣu । maraṇāśanisaṃnipātabhītāḥ giridurgeṣv aparāyaṇā vasāmaḥ ।। rajasāpi virūkṣitātmabhāvāḥ paruṣaiś copahatā gadaprahāraiḥ । mahatīm api yātanāṃ vahante vacanatrāsajaḍā bhavanti mṛtyoḥ ।।
hariṇo hariṇeva bandhumadhyād abhibhūya prasabhaṃ vikṛṣyamāṇaḥ । avikhaṇḍitapauruṣeṇa mṛtyudviṣatā duḥkham ayaṃ paraiti lokaḥ ।। pariśuṣkagalāntarālanāḍāḥ saritāṃ prāpya taṭāny udanvatīnām । anavāptajalā mṛgāribhītā vayam utplutya diśo diśaṃ vrajāmaḥ ।।
śaṣpodbhedapracayaharitān saṃparityajya dāvān । śārdūlānāṃ nakhamukhaśikhālakṣyabhāvaṃ vrajāmaḥ ।। tṛṇapuruṣakān apy ālokya dravanti manāṃsi no na niśi na divā mṛtyor bhītāḥ sukhāni labhāmahe । vitatadhanuṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyādhaṃ kṛtāntam ivāparaṃ na bhavati bhayatrastāṅgānāṃ manāg api bhojanam ।। tarupallavāharitapāṭalādharāḥ kṣitireṇudhūsaritaromarājikāḥ ।
hariṇāṅganā na ramayanti no mano maraṇāturaṃ prakṛticañcalekṣaṇāḥ ।। salīlaṃ kāntābhiḥ saha gamanavinyāsacaturāḥ । prayatnād vadhyante tad api hariṇā raudramatibhiḥ ।। aṭatām aṭavīṣv avāritānāṃ tṛṇaśaṣpāṅkuramātrabhojanānām ।
vada kaṃ nu samīkṣya vairibhāvaṃ hariṇānām api vidviṣo bhavanti ।। ṛjuṣūttānacitteṣu tṛṇatoyopajīviṣu । hariṇeṣu kathaṃ krūrāḥ praharanti mṛgadviṣaḥ ।। sarvaduḥkhapratikruṣṭaṃ sarvabhūtabhayaṃkaram ।
avaimi maraṇaṃ tasmād upasargaduruttaram ।। yataś ca te mahāsattvāḥ svaṃ svaṃ vādam abhiniviṣṭā na kathāparyavasānam āsādayanti tato bodhisattvam upetya nyāyataḥ praṇamyemam artham ūcuḥ । bhagavan kṣudrāgakrodhamaraṇabhayānāṃ kiṃ nu duḥkham । kasya vāsmākaṃ subhāṣitam ity athainān sa munivaryo abravīt । subhāṣitaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ ca suniścitam । sarvāṇy etāni duḥkhāni rujanti bhuvanatrayam ।।
api ca bhadramukhā mamāpy abhiprāyaḥ śrūyatām । abhīkṣṇasamudācāro dharme yo yasya bādhate । āśramaṃ manaso duḥkham ity avaimi bravīmi ca ।। spardhamānā ivānyonyam upaghnanti vidāhinaḥ ।
lokān eva nirālokāñ janmasaṃbandhino malāḥ ।। kṣudduḥkhopahatātmānaḥ kiṃ na kuryuḥ śarīriṇaḥ । apāyaphalasaṃdhānadāruṇaṃ karmavaiśasam ।। vyatikrāntāryamaryādā rāgopakliṣṭacetasaḥ ।
bhavanti karuṇāpātraṃ puruṣās tattvadarśinām ।। sphuṭabhrūbhaṅgavikṣepabhramadvikṛtalocanāḥ । kṣaṇenānya ivābhānti puruṣāḥ paruṣā ruṣā ।। sarvasattvair vinābhāvapravāso dīrghakālikaḥ ।
bhayam ātyantikaṃ hīdaṃ maraṇaṃ sarvadehinām ।। ete cānye ca ye duḥkhaprakārā romaharṣaṇāḥ । te jātim anuvartante karuṇām iva sādhavaḥ ।। mātāpitror vipratipattiṃ ।
kiṃ nāma tataḥ paraṃ duḥkham ।। ।। । kiṃ nāma tataḥ paraṃ duḥkham ।।
ruddhocchvāsasya bhṛśaṃ kṛmer ivāmedhyapaṅkamagnasya । yā garbhasthasya daśā kiṃ nāma tataḥ paraṃ duḥkham ।। kāyāvaskaranirjharavivare niṣpiṣyamāṇadehasya । yā prasavasthasya daśā kiṃ nāma tataḥ paraṃ duḥkham ।।
tasmāj jātiṃ duḥkhaṃ jātijarāvyādhimaraṇanirmuktāḥ । kathayanti kathikavarā jinā jitakathaṃkathābījāḥ ।। pradhvaṃsavyasanaṃ mahātyayam asatsaṃparkajaṃ vaikṛtam । jātiṃ prāpya yato bhavanti jagataḥ saiveha duḥkhaṃ tataḥ ।।
sarvākāraparopakāramadhurā yeṣāṃ samutpattayaḥ । janma svārthaparasya tu kṣaṇikam apy āpāyikī viplutiḥ ।। tasmād brūmahe । saṃbodhaye kuruta vā sthiram apramādaṃ tūrṇaṃ ghaṭadhvam atha vā bhavasaṃkṣayāya ।
etad dvayaṃ tu virahayya viśanty akāmā bhīmāny apāyavaḍavāmukhagahvarāṇi ।। yatnena ced ubhayam etad avāpnuvanti yatnaḥ phale mahati yuktataro mato me । chidraṃ varāṭakam avāpya sudhāpi kiṃ syāc cintāmaṇer adhigamāya varaṃ śramo api ।। māṃ praty ataś ca viphalo api varaṃ prayāsaḥ sādhor mahājanahitāvahitāśayasya ।
icchāviśeṣaviṣayasya parākramasya prasthānam eva mahatīṃ ratim ādadhāti ।। sādhāraṇāni dayitaiḥ saha pelavāni āmodayanti sutarāṃ hṛdayaṃ sukhāni । pīḍākarāṇi mahatāṃ samupasthitāni prākarṣikāny api sukhāni tu yautakāni ।। dīptir nāsau sphurati jagatāṃ ।
arthāvāptir vinayanakṛśā nāsti sātulyarūpā ।। ājñāṃ śirobhir atha te pratigṛhya tasya mānābhimānamṛdubhir munisattamasya । dharmaikatānamanasaḥ prathayāṃ babhūvuḥ kīrtiṃ śaratkumudinīdhavalāṃ samantāt ।। iti ṛṣipañcakajātakam ।।
oṃ namo ratnatrayāya ।। vairāgyayuktaṃ ca subhāṣitaṃ ca dharmārthakāmapratibodhanaṃ ca । ekāntaramyaṃ bahusajjanānāṃ vakṣyāmi kiṃ cic chṛṇutāvadānam ।। evam idaṃ bhrājet paripakvakuśalamūlānāṃ mahānto api bhogā yauvanaṃ vā nālam antarāyāyeti ।
tadyathānuśrūyate । nayavinayādiguṇaśrīsamṛddho rājābhūt kṛkī nāma । sa ca bhagavati kāśyape samyaksaṃbuddhe samupajātaprasādaḥ । tasya rājñaḥ sapta kumāryaḥ pūrvabuddhotpādasaṃniropitābhivṛddhakuśalamūlabalādhānāḥ samupajātasaṃsāravāsanirvedās tāḥ savinayopacāraṃ madhureṇa vacasā praṇipatya pitaram abruvan । kāmān kruddhabhujaṅgabhogapaṭalacchāyopamān vīkṣya ca । naiṣkramyābhiratāśayāḥ khalu vayaṃ yāmaḥ śmaśānaṃ nṛpa ।।
rājovāca ।। bālāḥ sukhocitā yūyam akṛtārthamanorathāḥ । kathaṃ śaknomy ahaṃ vaktum āśrayadhvaṃ tapovanam ।। kanyakā ūcuḥ ।
jānīmahe kṣitipate bhavato jane api snehārdrapeśalarasābhiniveṣṭitāni । asmāsu kiṃ punar akāraṇavatsalasya svāṅke vivṛddhim anaghāṃ samupāgatāsu ।। yuṣmadvidhair api sahābhimukho viyogo yenaiva no nṛpa niratyayaśuddhabhāvaiḥ । tenaiva śāntipadam āptum iyaṃ manīṣā mā bhūt punaḥ punar ayaṃ vyasanopatāpaḥ ।।
atha sa rājā snehavaśād vitānībhūtahṛdayo niścalābhitāmranayanayugalaḥ punaḥ punas tāḥ kanyakāḥ samabhivīkṣyovāca ।। āstīrṇakomalavicitrakuthodareṣu svairaṃ vihṛtya bhavaneṣu kathaṃ bhavatyaḥ । sprakṣyanti durjanamanoviṣamāṃ śmaśānabhūmiṃ sitāsthiśakalaprakarottarīyām ।। snehonmukhaṃ pitaram ekapade kathaṃ vā śokāśrudurdinamukhīṃ jananīṃ ca hitvā ।
amlānasauhṛdanirantaramānasāṃś ca tyaktvā kathaṃ nu suhṛdas tapase ramadhvam ।। atha tāḥ kanyakā niratiśayadhairyāvaṣṭambhagalbhaṃ pitaram ūcuḥ । mātā pitā suhṛd iti vyavahāramātram etat punarbhavanipātavighātabhājām । bhūtārthadarśanaparokṣamalīmasānāṃ loko vṛthā narapate parikhedam eti ।।
kenāpy anartharucinā kapaṭaṃ prayuktam etat suhṛtsvajanabandhumayaṃ vicitram । kasyātra kaḥ katham iha svajano jano vā svapnendrajālasadṛśaḥ khalu jīvalokaḥ ।। yāvad buddhadivākarasya vilasatkīrtiprabhāmālinaḥ । tāvan nyāyyam ataḥ purā hy atimahat paryeti ghoraṃ tamaḥ ।।
niryāntaṃ na nivārayanti puruṣaṃ tacchāntikāmā yathā । niṣkrāmantam anarthajālapihitāt santo vivṛṇvanti na ।। atha sa pārthivas tāsāṃ tena suhṛtsvajanabandhunirapekṣarūkṣākṣareṇa svakāyajīvitāśāvidhureṇa vacasā sutarāṃ samupajātaśokadainyamānasaḥ punar vyāha ।। tapāṃsy akāleṣv abhivāñchitāni puṣṇanti nārthān manaso anukūlān akālagarbhā iva kanyakānām ajātasārāvayavāṅgaśobhāḥ ।।
bhavanty akāle tapasaḥ prayogāś candroparāgā iva sopasargāḥ । tasmād ito buddhir iyaṃ kumāryo nivartyatām utpathacāriṇīva ।। soḍhuṃ na duḥkhāni vapūṃṣi śaktāny adṛṣṭaduḥkhāni sukhocitāni । dantābhighātā dviradādhipānām abaddhamūlā iva cūtavṛkṣāḥ ।।
savahnigarbhair aśivaiḥ śivārutair vināditaṃ bhīṣaṇarāvagahvaram । bhayaṃ bhayasyāpy upasaṃhared bhṛśaṃ śmaśānam ākrandavirāvadāruṇam ।। kva vo vapur bālamṛṇālakomalaṃ matiḥ kva ceyaṃ karapattraniṣṭhurā । paropakāravyatiṣaktacetaso vidher aho mayy anapekṣarūkṣatā ।।
vaiḍūryanīlamṛduśādvalakañcukāni nānāprakārakusumaprakarotkarāṇi । etāni vo madakalālikulākulāni krīḍāvanāny abhimatāni bhavantu kanyāḥ ।। samīraṇacalattaraṅgarucakāvalīmekhalāḥ । rater upanibandhanaṃ maghavato apy alaṃ kanyakāḥ ।।
upavījitā jalataraṅgalāsakair navamālikākusumagandhagandhibhiḥ । pavanair ihaiva gṛhakānane ratiṃ kurutāṅganāḥ parabhṛtopakūjite ।। nānāmodavidigdhavāsavikasanniḥśvāsavātā iva । yuṣmākaṃ rataye bhavantu vanitāḥ saṃgītatūryasvanāḥ ।।
atha tāḥ kumāryas tat pitur vacanam amṛṣyamāṇāḥ punar vyāhuḥ ।। na hi tat sukham asti kiṃ cid anyan naralokādhipate divi kṣitau vā । śataśaś ca sahasradhā ca bhuktaṃ na yad asmābhir anarthapaṇḍitābhiḥ ।। viṣayair na hi tṛptir indriyāṇāṃ viṣayābhyāsaviśeṣaghasmarāṇām ।
bhavatīti vicintya buddhimantaḥ prayatante bhavabandhanakṣayāya ।। capalāny anavasthitasvabhāvāny aniloddhūtataraṅgabhaṅgurāṇi । vinivṛttapunarbhavābhilāṣā vijayante yatayaḥ ṣaḍindriyāṇi ।। bhavacārakasūkarās tu bālāś chalitāś cittakaler viceṣṭitena ।
prapatanti sukhābhilāṣalubdhā vyasaneṣv eva durantabhairaveṣu ।। aham ity upajātavibhrameyaṃ janatā prajvalitāstrayantrakalpān । viṣayān upasevate hatāśā pariṇāmāyatatīvraduḥkhahetūn ।। jagad adhruvam etad asvatantraṃ viṣayāśīviṣapūgasaṃniruddham ।
avagamya bhaveṣu ye ramante paśavas te naravigrahopanītāḥ ।। camarā iva vṛkṣalagnavālā nidhanaṃ kāpuruṣā vrajanti gehe । viṣayair uparuddhabuddhimārgā vitathasnehalatānibaddhacittāḥ ।। ratikāraṇam atra jīvaloke vyasanodbhedanirantarāntarāle ।
vada tāta kim asti yena naḥ syād bhavaneṣv eva ratir bahucchaleṣu ।। bhavaneṣu narendra bhāgadheyāny upayujyāni bhavāntarārjitāni । muṣitā iva hīnadīnacittā bhavakāntāraparāyaṇā bhavanti ।। puruṣāḥ prasamīkṣya kāriṇo api vyavahāreṣu vicakṣaṇāḥ prakṛtyā ।
gṛhacārakam etya yānti nāśaṃ nṛpa mīnāḥ kupinīmukhaṃ yathaiva ।। bahubhir naralokapāla yatnair bhavanāni draviṇāni cārjitāni । apahāya naraḥ kṣaṇena yāti svakṛtādeśitamārga eka eva ।। ata eva jagāda lokanātho nṛpa karmasvakam eva jīvalokam ।
maraṇābhimukhaṃ naraṃ svakarma stanapo vatsa ivānuyāti dhenum ।। tad alaṃ pariṇāmadāruṇais taiḥ priyabandho priyasaṃgamābhilāṣaiḥ । dhruvam eva hi viprayogaduḥkhaṃ priyasaṃyogaratāśayā labhante ।। api cāpariniṣṭhitasvabhāve priyatā kā naravīra jīvaloke ।
paramārthavicārapelavānāṃ priya ity eva hi vibhramo matīnām ।। yadi tu priyatāsti kā cid asmāsv anujānīṣva mahīpate tato asmān । anavadyam ahāryam āryajuṣṭaṃ sukham āsvādayituṃ hi no manīṣā ।। atha sa rājā sugataśāsanābhiprasanno dharmāntarāyabhīrur jātasnehākrāntahṛdayaḥ svā duhitṝḥ pūrvajanmānusmaraṇāvagamitaprayojanā jātismarāḥ khalv etā iti parivicintya suciraṃ tūṣṇīṃ babhūva ।।
nirbandham iti vijñāya tāsāṃ sa narapuṅgavaḥ । gacchatety aparivyaktaṃ kathaṃ cid anujajñivān ।। atha tā dārikā vyapanītasraganulepanābharaṇāḥ vinayanibhṛtavapuṣaḥ sitasūkṣmapralambāmbaradharāḥ pavanabalacalitasalilaphenāvalīmālinya iva saritaḥ sāndracandracandrikāpaṭāvaguṇṭhitā iva śaranniśāḥ svakiraṇajālottarīyā iva saptarṣitārakāḥ krameṇa viracitacitāgnimadhyavinyastasimisimāyamānocchūnaśavāmagandhabībhatsaṃ niśitagṛdhratuṇḍakhaṇḍitaśiroghaṭīvivaravinirgatavigalitamastiṣkarasaviliptavadananarakaraṅkākrāntaparyantabhīṣaṇaṃ jīrṇaśīrṇavivarṇāsthikaṅkālaśakalanikarakharabhūmibhāgaduḥsaṃcaraṃ mūrtimantam iva nirvedakarmāntam ivāntakasyāratiśokadainyopāyāsāspadabhūtaṃ śmaśānam anuprāptāḥ ।। vyāluptāntrodarārdrair aratibhayakaraiḥ saṃniruddhaṃ śavāṅgaiḥ ।
jīrṇanyagrodharandhravyavahitavividholūkahūṅkārabhīmam ।। kva cit sitakaraṅkajālapariṇaddhaduḥsaṃcaram । nilīnabahumakṣikāśataśavākulopatyakam ।। sphuratsphuṭacitāgniśuṣkatarumūlalīnoragam ।
mahānasam ivāntakasya satatapravṛttotsavam ।। vasāsavavikāraghasmarapiśācipūgākulam । sphurannarakalevarodaravinirgatāntroragam ।। saṃvegānaddhahṛdayā vicerus tatra tāḥ striyaḥ ।
svabhāvaṃ jīvalokasya cintayantyaś calācalam ।। vivṛtavikṛtapūtiguhyadeśaṃ dharaṇirajo'ruṇarūkṣakeśapāśam । khaganakhamukhakhaṇḍitākṣikośaṃ dadṛśur athojjhitam aṅganāyāḥ ।। muhur upāgatasādhvasacañcalaiḥ kuvalayāvayavair iva locanaiḥ ।
tam abhivīkṣya kalevarapañjaraṃ bahuvidhāni vacāṃsi babhāṣire ।। iyam asau sphuṭacandrakarāṅkuracchuritasaudhavimānanivāsinī । priyatamāṅkapariṣvajanocitā svapiti yā vasudhātalamaṇḍale ।। priyabhujāntarapañjaraśāyikā jaladharastaniteṣv api kātarā ।
sadahanād aśivāc ca śivārutāt katham iyaṃ na bibheti tapasvinī ।। gurunitambabharālasagāminī lalitahāsavilāsavilokinī । iyam asau svagṛhāṅganacandrikā gataghṛṇair vihagair avalupyate ।। narakaraṅkaśatākulacatvare pitṛvane bhagini tvam ihojjhitā ।
akaruṇena kathaṃ dayitena he dhig anavasthitahārdam idaṃ jagat ।। svajanabandhusuhṛtkamalākarabhramarikā dayitāṅkavivartinī । katham iyaṃ kṣaṇadācarabhairave pitṛvane ramate adya varākikā ।। kāntaṃ snigdhavidagdhamugdhamadhureṇodīkṣamāṇā purā ।
saṃtrāsaṃ vihagāpanītanayanā kaṣṭaṃ karoty aṅganā ।। antarnigūḍhavividhāśucigātrayaṣṭyā rāgāndhabuddhinayanāś chalitā mayeti । saṃrāgiṇo apahasatīva khagāvaluptadantacchadena vadanena varāṅganeyam ।। nidrāṃ bheje priyatamapariṣvaṅgaviśrabdhagarbhām ।
gomāyūnāṃ dhvanitamukharārāvaraudre śmaśāne ।। vālāgramātram api yatra vicāryamāṇe nekṣāmahe śuci nijāśucigarbharandhre । tasmin ratiṃ katham amī prakhalā labhante kāyādhame nidhanadharmiṇi roganīḍe ।। svapnendrajālajalacandracalasvabhāvam ।
prāṇāvaśeṣam upayāti na vo vināśam ।। prāṇāntikavyasanakaṇṭakabhinnamarmā kurvīta kiṃ nu kuśalaṃ jalaviplutākṣaḥ । daṣṭaḥ kṛtāntamakareṇa jarāmukhena mūrdhnā ca śuklapalitotkaradantureṇa ।। ghorāndhakāraparalokamahāprapātasaṃpātacūrṇitatanoḥ kuśalābhilāṣam ।
āśīviṣāsyapuṭasaṃkaṭasaṃniruddhamaṇḍūkavāsitasamaṃ pravadanti santaḥ ।। dhatse kasmāt paruṣapiśunābaddhavādapragalbhaiḥ । jihvāpeśīṃ harati vihagas tuṇḍasaṃdaṃśakena ।। yad bālānāṃ nayanaviṣayaṃ prāpya dhairyaṃ bibheda ।
nāryā gṛdhrā nakhamukhapadanyāsapaṅktiṃ likhanti ।। bhittau sācīpariṇatamukhī citram udvīkṣamāṇā । tāv evādya grasati caraṇau jambuko ayaṃ yuvatyāḥ ।। kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭaṃ madanamadirāḥ kṣībacittāḥ patanti ।
nirvidyadhvaṃ pracalitataḍidbhaṅgurāj jīvalokāt ।। saṃtaptānām adhigatayathābhūtadharmādhirājaḥ । śāstre tasmai paramabhiṣaje sarvakāle namo astu ।। sarvākāraṃ vivṛtam akhilaṃ yena janmābhidhānam ।
lokas tīvravyasanakuliśāghātaniṣpiṣṭamūrtiḥ ।। yasmin kānto maṇimakarikāṃ yauvanāgre babandha । kaṣṭaṃ dhṛṣṭaḥ spṛśati balibhuk tac chiro adyāṅganāyāḥ ।। ye vāsitāḥ sukusumena vivāhakāle mātuḥ kareṇa kṛtakautukamaṅgalena ।
te adya pracaṇḍapavanair avadhūyamānāḥ keśāḥ śmaśānatarucāmaratāṃ prayātāḥ ।। salalitapadanyāsā kvāsau gatir madavihvalā । suracitam aho citraṃ māyārahasyam idaṃ kaleḥ ।। yasmin prāṇasamaś cakāra muditaḥ pattrāṅkuraṃ yatnataḥ ।
vaktraṃ raktakalaṅkitaṃ nikaṣati sthitvā lalāṭe aṇḍajaḥ ।। vistīrṇastanacakravākayugale vakṣastaḍāgodare । petus tatra vipūyake adya nipatanty āśātikā makṣikāḥ ।। preṣyābhir valayadhvanivyatikaraiḥ saṃvījitā sundarī ।
tām evādya tu vījayanti paruṣaiḥ pakṣānilair vāyasāḥ ।। yenāyaṃ kampitaḥ pūrvaṃ śākhāntaravicāriṇā । kvemaṃ kāyadrumaṃ tyaktvā sa gataś cittamarkaṭaḥ ।। yena niṣkriyam apy etat kriyāvad iva lakṣyate ।
kalevaram anātmīyaṃ kva sa cittavidūṣakaḥ ।। antarātmānam icchanti yam avidyāndhabuddhayaḥ । vijñānadhūrtakaḥ kvāsau gatas tīrthavimohakaḥ ।। ciraṃ vyāmohitaṃ yena na tattveṣu pratiṣṭhitam ।
jagat kva nu prayāto asmāc cittacitrendrajālikaḥ ।। na jānanti gatiṃ yasya kapilādyās tapodhanāḥ । cittavidyādharaḥ kvāsau viṣayāmbaragocaraḥ ।। cacāra yo asminn aśucau navadvāre calācale ।
śarīrapañjare so adya kva nu cittavihaṅgamaḥ ।। tīvracchidravyasananivahakṣāravāriprapūrṇe । yātas tyaktvā kva nu tanum imāṃ cittanaktaṃcaro asau ।। sphuradvahnijvālāvalayakapiladvāravivare ।
kva yāto asāv asmāt prakṛticapalaś cittaturagaḥ ।। savinayam upagamya prītivispanditākṣaḥ । prakṛtisubhagavācā vāsavaḥ kanyakās tāḥ ।। nṛpatikulavibhūtiśrīsukhaṃ paryudasya ।
vratam idam iti tuṣṭo asmy adya vaḥ kiṃ vṛṇīdhvam ।। tridaśapatisukhaṃ vā niścayasyāsya vo adya । sphurati manasi yad vo devarājo asmi śakraḥ ।। prakṛtirucirabhāvās tiryag ālokya śakram ।
svakuśalaparipākāṅgāradhīrasvabhāvaḥ ।। na vayam amarabandho janmaduḥkhāturatvād bhavasukhalavalolāt tantusaṃtānaneyāḥ । vratam idam anubaddhāḥ śokabāṣpāmbuleśaiḥ kaluṣavadanaśobhān bāndhavān apy apāsya ।। vyasanaśatasahasrāghātanirbhidyamānam । padam abhayam aśokaṃ prāptum abhyudyatāḥ smaḥ ।।
yadi jagadanukampāpeśalādhyāśayatvāt । bhavabhayaparitaptāḥ prāpayāsmān vimokṣam ।। niryāṇāsthikaṭāhakārpitaśirā mūrcchāturo niṣpatan । duḥkhaṃ duḥkhaparaṃparāṃ ca paratas tāṃ chinddhi jātiṃ hi naḥ ।।
jarā rakṣoyoṣit palitasitadaṃṣṭrāṅkuravatī । tatas trāyasvāsmān prabhavasi yadi tvaṃ surapate ।। saṃprāptān api bhoktum apratibalo bhogān vicitrojjvalān । trātā no bhava mṛtyudūtapuruṣād ditsur varaṃ ced bhavān ।।
kṣobhāyāsapratihatatanuḥ śītaviṣṭabdhagātraḥ । yenāghrāto vrajati vilayaṃ pāhi mṛtyos tato asmān ।। kāryākāryavibhāgapelavamatir nindāspadaṃ jāyate । tan no rāgahutāśanaṃ varada he nirvāpayāpāyikam ।।
pāpāḥ pāpaṃ narakam aśivaṃ kurvate tatkṣaṇena । tan naḥ śakra vyapanaya manaḥkoṭarāt krodhasarpam ।। mithyādṛṣṭiviṣopadigdhamanaso mārgāntaraṃ saṃśritāḥ । tan naś chindhi manogṛhāntaracaraṃ mohāndhakāraṃ hare ।।
varam evaṃvidhaṃ śakra bhavantaṃ prārthayāmahe । pratijñātārthavidhuraṃ ceṣṭante na hi sādhavaḥ ।। atha śakras tena tāsāṃ viṣayaprārthanākārpaṇyānapekṣāsvacchaśobhinā vacasā pravijṛmbhamāṇavismayaḥ prasādasaṃhṛṣitatanūruhaḥ prāha । aśakyam arthaṃ khalu yācyamāno vighātadīnatvam upaiti lokaḥ ।
varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ naradevakanyā yad eva śakyeta mayā pradātum ।। atha tā dārikās tena tasyāntarnigūḍhaśāṭhyavikalpitena vacasā samupajātasaṃvegāmarṣāḥ śakram ūcuḥ । upalāpayase kimartham asmān upagamyādya sahasralocanaivam । sukhamātrakadurvidagdhabuddhe prakhalās tena vayaṃ na cāpi gamyāḥ ।।
vidito bhavato na rājavaṃśaḥ kim asau dikṣu vikīrṇakīrtipuñjaḥ । dhanado apy ayathārthanāmadheyo dhanasāraṃ samavekṣya yasya nūnam ।। yam apāsya vayaṃ jarārtimṛtyuvyasanāyāsavighātadainyabhītāḥ । suranātha daśām imāṃ prapannā na bhayān nāpi ca bālacāpalena ।।
kṛtapuṇya viheṭhitābhir arthas tava ko asmābhir atīva duḥkhitābhiḥ । upajīva sabandhumitrabhṛtyo vibhavan nanda ca śakra dīrgharātram ।। sukṛtojjvalabhāgadheyayogād yadi devādhipatir bhavāṃs tataḥ kim । na hi saṃpadam āpnuvanti santaḥ paraheṭhākaraṇāya devarāja ।।
atha mahendras tāsāṃ sphuṭavicitramahārthasārasūcakair vacobhir āpyāyitavismayaḥ prasādābhivyajyamānavadanaśobhaḥ punar api bhāvajijñāsur arthāntarātiśayaśuśrūṣayā vācātyuvāca । mā tāvad bhaginyaḥ nāthante darśanasyāpi mama loke tapodhanāḥ । kimartham evaṃ varade mayi yūyaṃ tu niṣṭhurāḥ ।। atha tāḥ kumāryaḥ punar abhyadhikatarajanitamanyukopāḥ sāmarṣaṃ rūkṣākṣaraṃ tridaśapatim ūcuḥ ।
anyathaiva sitāpāṅgamukhasmitavilokitam । dṛśyate vadanaṃ śacyā dīyate varam anyathā ।। varapradāne yady asti śaktis tava purandara । jahīhi prakhalāṃ tāvad viṣayāśāpiśācikām ।।
athavā dustyajāḥ kāmā mithyāsaṃkalpalolupaiḥ । ta eva santu te nityāḥ prabhāvo asti yadīdṛśaḥ ।। adhruveṣu sahasrākṣa kāmeṣv āsaktamānasaḥ । varaṃ vada kathaṃ nāma tvam anyasmai pradāsyasi ।।
uhyamānaḥ kathaṃ nāma saritā bhīmavegayā । uttārayiṣyasy aparān parikṣāmajaḍāśrayaḥ ।। pāṃśukūlāmbaradharā vyapanītaśiroruhāḥ । araṇyād grāmam eṣyāmaḥ kadā nas tad bhaviṣyati ।।
yugamātravilokinyo mṛtpātravyagrapāṇayaḥ । sāvadhānaṃ kadā bhikṣāṃ cariṣyāmaḥ kulāt kulam ।। asaktā lābhasatkārapaṅke saṃkleśasaṃkaṭe । kadā viśodhayiṣyāmo deyadharmānurāgiṇaḥ ।।
palālapuñjād utthāya nīhāragurucīvarāḥ । yatheccham annapānārthe yāsyāmo niḥspṛhāḥ kadā ।। taror mūle śukaśyāme mṛduśādvalakañcuke । kadā niṣadya prāpsyāmo dṛṣṭadharmasukhotsavam ।।
kāyajīvitayos tyaktvā jarattṛṇalaveṣv iva । apekṣāṃ sucirābhyastāḥ kadā lapsyāmahe sukham ।। kadā sarinnikuñjasthās taraṅgair udayavyayam । ujjhāmo jīvalokasya bhidyamānair muhur muhuḥ ।।
satkāyadṛṣṭim utpāṭya sarvātmadṛṣṭimātrikām । niḥspṛhā bhavabhogebhyo bhaviṣyāmaḥ kadā vayam ।। avabhotsyāmahe lokaṃ kadā nu sacarācaram । svapnamāyāmarīcyabhragandharvanagaropamam ।।
iti yāsāṃ priyā trātaḥ spṛhā hṛdi vijṛmbhate vareṇa tāsāṃ ko nv arthaḥ sāmiṣeṇa calena ca ।। api ca sureśāna varapradānacittaka । mithyāvikalpakṣaṇamātraramyāḥ svabhāvavāmāḥ suranātha kāmāḥ । vivarjitāḥ sadbhir udāracittair mahāprapātā iva sāndhakārāḥ ।।
sarvānayopadravahetubhūtāḥ kāmāḥ khalīkārakarā narāṇām । jugupsitāś caiva bhayāvahāś ca purīṣadigdhā iva kṛṣṇasarpāḥ ।। yān sevamānā nidhanaṃ prayātāḥ prayānti yāsyanti ca sattvakāyāḥ । tān vadhyaghātapratimān bhajeta ko nāma kāmān aghahetubhūtān ।।
śakre ca ye pāṃśupiśācake ca surendra tulyaṃ dadhati svabhāvam । asadvikalpapraṇayodbhavatvāt seved dhi kāmān manasāpi kas tān ।। vaiḍūryanīlaharitodgataśādvalāni tyaktvā vanāni kusumonmiṣitadrumāṇi । tīkṣṇāṅkuśollikhitajarjarakumbhadeśā bhārān vahanti viṣayaiś chalitā gajendrāḥ ।।
śūlāntalagnavapuṣaḥ parivījyamānāḥ pakṣānilair nagaravāyasamaṇḍalānām । vyājena mitranayanair abhivīkṣyamāṇā nāśaṃ vrajanti puruṣā viṣayāhidaṣṭāḥ ।। prajvālya kāmadahanaṃ svayam eva bālā mithyāvikalpapavanaiḥ svamanogṛheṣu । ātmānam eva hi dahanti śaracchatāni saṃgharṣajena dahanena yathaiva vaṃśāḥ ।।
api ca kuliśapāṇe vaijayante vihṛtya sphuritamaṇimarīciśrīsamunmeṣaramye । jvaladanalakarālāṃ yānti bhūyo apy avīciṃ yadi viṣayaviṣaktāḥ svasti tasmai sukhāya ।। cyavanapatanaduḥkhaklībalolekṣaṇas tu । nanu sukham anubhūtaṃ tena pūrvānubhūtam ।।
yadi surapuravāpyāṃ ratnanaubhir vigāhya । kvathitanarakaraṅkavyākulāntarjalāyām ।। surabhavanasukhebhyaḥ kā spṛhā śakra tebhyaḥ । sakalam iti viditvā mokṣakāmāḥ sthitāḥ smaḥ ।।
bhavagatigahanāntarvartināṃ bāliśānām । sakalam api yato asmān sarvaduḥkhaprasūtiḥ ।। bhavati yad api saukhyaṃ kākatālīyam asmin । salilam iva nadīnāṃ prāpya sāmudram ambhaḥ ।।
kiṃcitsthānaṃ kalitavalayaiś candanāśleṣaśītaiḥ । nidrāṃ prāpya vyajanapavanavyastamālopahāraḥ ।। bhūyaḥ śete klamagurutanur darbhasūcīkarāle mārge bhasmavyatikarakharair vījyamāno marudbhiḥ । tasmān matvā kṣaṇasukhalavaṃ cañcalaṃ jīvalokaṃ tyaktvā kāmān vyasanaphaladān brahmaśāntaṃ bhajeta ।। gosk । daśaśatanayano atha kanyakānāṃ hṛṣitatanūruhakañcuko vacobhiḥ ।
vyavasitam abhinandya caiva tāsāṃ tridaśapurābhimukho yayau kṣaṇena ।। pravrajyām atha samupetya tāḥ kumāryas tattvārthapravicayaśuddhabuddhinetrāḥ । utterur madavirasaṃ calattaraṅgaṃ saṃsāravyasanamahārṇavaṃ durantam ।। sarvārthaprakṛtivibhāganiścitātmā sarvebhyo munir itivṛttakaṃ jagāda ।
mohāndhe jagati samantacakṣur ekaṃ sattvebhyo bhavabhayakaṇṭakakṣatebhyaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīsaptakumārikāvadānaṃ samāptam ।। ।। kṛtir ācāryabhadantagopadattasya ।। jarattṛṇānīva śarīrakāṇy api tyajanti santo na ca līnamānasāḥ ।
kṛpājalakṣālitadehamatsarā jagadvipattijvalanopaśāntaye ।। tadyathānuśrūyate । bodhisattvabhūtaḥ kila bhagavān saṃtoṣābhyāsād apagatabhavopabhogaviśeṣābhilāṣaḥ suparijñātasaṃskārasvabhāvatvāt svadehe apy astamitasnehānubandhas tṛṣṇādoṣapratyakṣajñānatayā tadabhidheyamānaso janmāntarābhyastavividhalābhakuśalatvād upāyāntareṇāpi dhanārjanasamarthaḥ samupacitapuṇyasambhāratayā cābhiprāyamātreṇāpi draviṇavibhūtyākarṣaṇaprabhuḥ prabhūtavittopakaraṇo api san kevalam udadhigatajagadvyasanoparitrāṇāyavia saṃketapracārasāṃyātrikaparivṛto mahāsamudram upajagāma । athāvagāḍhāḥ payasāṃ nidhānaṃ gambhīrabhīmāyatapaṅktirandhram ।
velācalopaghnaviśīrṇaphenasitāntalekhaṃ vaṇijaḥ krameṇa ।। tatkarmabhir vā pariṇāmaraudraiḥ svabhāvato vāmbunidhiḥ kṣaṇena । paryādadāno hṛdayāni teṣāṃ saṃvartakālādhikadāruṇo abhūt ।। kharamakarakarāgracchinnabālapravāladrumarasaparibhogāpāṭalāvartacakram ।
viyad iva navasaṃdhyārañjitāmbhodajālaṃ salilanidhim udīkṣya trāsamūkās ta āsan ।। vanam iva kumudānāṃ dhautam indor mayūkhair viṣamitasitaphenacchedavinyāsacitram । lavaṇasalilarāśiṃ vīkṣamāṇāḥ samantān na ratim upayayus te prāṇasaṃdehakāle ।। vivṛtadaśanaśaṅkhadhvānavitrastamīno bhujagabhuvanaśṛṅgaprāntabhinnormijālaḥ ।
hṛdayam udadhir alpasthāma teṣāṃ bibheda sphuritavikṛtanakrākrāntavistīrṇakukṣiḥ ।। anilabalavibhaktaiḥ śailatuṅgais taraṅgair nabha iva nigirantaṃ sārkanakṣatracandram । tam udadhim avalokya prāṇasaṃdehadolāṃ kṛpaṇakamanasas te sarva evādhirūḍhāḥ ।। bhujagam iva viṣāgnicchedamālākarālaṃ śvasanavikacabhogaṃ kruddham udvīkṣamāṇāḥ । lavaṇajalaniketaṃ taṃ durālokapāraṃ maraṇabhayaviṣaṇṇās te paraṃ moham īyuḥ ।।
nicayam iva ghanānāṃ vāribhārālasānāṃ timiram iva vamantaṃ vīcicūrṇapravegaiḥ । jalanidhim avagāḍhās te nirākrandabhīmaṃ muṣitavadanaśobhā bodhisattvaṃ praṇemuḥ ।। adṛṣṭapūrvair atha tannimittair bhayaṃkarair ākulitā vicitraiḥ । ity ūcur āgadgadadīnakaṇṭhās taṃ bodhisattvaṃ samudīkṣamāṇāḥ ।।
ayaṃ janas tvatpratibaddhasarvaprayojanāśāvinivṛttaceṣṭaḥ । yad atra kṛtyaṃ kriyatāṃ tad āśu prāṇātyayaḥ saṃprati vartate naḥ ।। nirīkṣamāṇasya puro janas te nirudyamo majjati toyarāśau । kālātipāto atra na yuktarūpaḥ parākramasva svabalena tasmāt ।।
tvatpādamūlānucaro na kaś cit saṃspṛṣṭapūrvo vyasanaiḥ kadā cit । trāyasva tasmād vipadāṃ mukheṣu bhramantam enaṃ naravīra lokam ।। piteva putrān anukampamānas tan no bhayān mṛtyukarodarasthān । vimocayāsmān paramāryasattva tvaṃ naḥ paritrāṇam upadravebhyaḥ ।।
na devatānām api bhūmayas tās tava prabhāvā na caranti yāsu । tad eṣa kālaḥ kṛpaṇān anāthān asmān paritrātum avandhyaśakte ।। manyāmahe tvaṃ samanusmṛto api trāṇaṃ paraṃ sarvajagadbhayebhyaḥ । prāg eva sākṣād abhivīkṣyamāṇas tat pauruṣaṃ darśaya lokabandho ।।
jighāṃsanti krūrāḥ pṛthuvivaravistīrṇajaṭharāḥ । paritrāyasvemaṃ nikaṭavinipātaṃ janam ataḥ ।। svapucchavicchinnataraṅgasaṃkalā niśātadantāntavilagnaśuktayaḥ । abhidravanty ārya purā timiṅgilā janān imāṃs tvaccaraṇāśritān api ।।
vilambituṃ nātha na yujyate adhunā viśīryate naur iyam ambutāḍitā । sphuranty amī vīra samantato jhaṣāḥ pramṛṣṭaguñjāphalaraktalocanāḥ ।। atha sa mahātmā tena durviṣaheṇa paravyasanenopataptamānasaḥ svaprāṇātyayam avigaṇayya niṣpratikāradāruṇāṃ tāṃ mahājanavyāpattim avetya kṛpāparigatātmā prakṛtidhīratayā tadavastho apy asaṃbhrāntacetās tatkālātiśayadhyāyinā vacasā tān sahāyān āśvāsayann abravīt । mṛtena sārdhaṃ na vasanti sāgarāḥ prasiddhir eṣām iyam eva śāśvatī ।
ato mamāśritya mṛtaṃ kaḍevaraṃ tarantu santo ambunidhiṃ sudustaram ।। saṃyuktasaṃyogam upetya sarve nirākulāḥ projjhya viṣādadainyam । ātmānam uttārayituṃ yatadhvaṃ mahārṇavān māṃ ca parārtipaṅkāt ।। āpadgatānāṃ suhṛdāṃ priyāṇāṃ cirānubaddhapraṇayāśayānām ।
ko anyo asty upāyo ramaṇīyarūpas tat kārṣṭa mā snehamayaṃ viṣādam ।। śatror api vyāpadam āpatantīṃ svaprāṇamūlyena nivārayeyam । prāg eva yuṣmākam analpakālasaṃvardhitasnehaparigrahāṇām ।। mamātmabhāvair apavṛttasaukhyaiḥ syāc cet sukhī kuntapipīliko api ।
jarattṛṇānīva tathāpi jahyām ahaṃ śarīrāṇi nirastakhedaḥ ।। trāṇāśayāyāṃ samupāśritānāṃ guṇaiḥ pavitrīkṛtamānasānām । hitāya dehaṃ tyajato mamaikaṃ dayāparītaṃ kim ivātra citram ।। parārthacaryāviguṇaṃ śarīraṃ vṛthā guruṃ bhāram ivodvahantaḥ ।
vrajanti khedaṃ pariśuddhasattvāḥ kṛpākalatrīkṛtajīvalokāḥ ।। evaṃvidhe yadi na kāyam imaṃ prayokṣye puṇyāgame nirupamānasukhānubandhe । ko artho amunā parihṛtena kaḍevareṇa vātāhatāmbunidhibudbudadurbalena ।। tyakṣyāmi nemaṃ yadi pūtikāyaṃ bhavaddhitādhānavidhānakāle ।
saṃtyājayiṣyaty abalaṃ balātmā jagadvināśāvahitaḥ kṛtāntaḥ ।। tyajāmi yuṣmān kim udīkṣamāṇo yaśo atha vā mānagataṃ ca dharmam । dehaṃ kalīnāṃ padabandhabhūtaṃ utāvaśo mṛtyukarābhimṛṣṭam ।। tad atra śokāya matir na deyā bhavadbhir āsannaparābhavāya ।
mama krameṇaiva samāgato ayaṃ mahotsavaḥ puṇyaviśeṣaramyaḥ ।। bahusukhalavanānātantusaṃtānaneyās tṛṇam iva gataśaṅkā deham ujjhanty asantaḥ । atisṛjati parārthaṃ kāyam āsannanāśaṃ yadi sucaritapūrvaṃ duṣkaraṃ kiṃ nu tatra ।। atha te puruṣās tena tasyādbhutenābhiprasāritamānasāḥ sutarāṃ tadviyogaśaṅkāvyathitahṛdayā viṣādadainyavidheyāś cintāviṣayātītagocaram aviṣahyam ativismayanīyaṃ ca tatkarma taṃ mahāsattvam aviratāśrudhārāprakṣālitanayanadīnavadanāḥ pādayoḥ saṃpariṣvajya praṇamya ca sarvāṅgair ity avadan ।
kāmam atraiva nidhanaṃ sarva eva mahodadhau । yāsyāmo na tu śakyāmaḥ kartum etad anāryakam ।। evaṃvidhasya vyasanāni dṛṣṭvā suhṛdviśeṣasya sudurlabhasya । prāṇair dhanair vā kim ihāsti kṛtyaṃ tat sāhasād vāraya dhīracetaḥ ।।
uttīrṇān api toyaughād asmān asmād duruttarāt । magnān duścaritāvarte kaḥ samuttārayiṣyati ।। nūnaṃ karmaṇa evāyaṃ vipākaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ । yenāpad iyam āyātā niṣpratīkāradāruṇā ।।
adhyupekṣya suhṛtpīḍām etāṃ pāpānubandhinīm । duḥkhāntam upayāsyāmaḥ kair upāyaiḥ punar vayam ।। dayāmṛdukasaṃtānaṃ kuryād antāvasāyinam । idaṃ karmāvadānaṃ te prāg evārya suhṛjjanam ।।
atha bodhisattvaḥ sutarāṃs tais teṣāṃ saujanyasūcakair vacobhiḥ pravijṛmbhamāṇatīvraprasādapremagauravakāruṇyas samanuneṣyaṃs tān sahāyakān anukampāmṛtavāribhiḥ siñcann iva tṛptivisargair ity abravīt । bhavadbhir anadhīṣṭo ahaṃ svabhūtyai dehasaṃjñakam । tyajāmy anarthaṃ tatra syād yuṣmākaṃ kim anāryakam ।। akāle kaumudī hy eṣā naivaitad vyasanaṃ mama ।
pratīkāro mayā labdho vipadām eṣa śāśvataḥ ।। sauhārdaviśrambhaniratyayā vo yady asti kā cin mayi cittavṛttiḥ । na kartum arhanti tato bhavanto dharmasya kīrtyābharaṇasya vighnam ।। cittaṃ balād api hite viniyojanīyam āryair anāryam ahitāc ca vivecanīyam ।
tasmāt pravṛttim iha karmaṇi sādhujuṣṭe nārhanti vighnayitum aśrumukhā bhavantaḥ ।। anupādānam evāsya parārthaṃ cāparigrahaḥ । māṃ saṃpratīkṣate kāyakale randhraprahāriṇaḥ ।। upātto apy ayam asmābhir anādeyo na nīyate ।
yadi sattvārthasācivyaṃ ko anenārthaḥ praṇāśinā ।। yadi nābhyuddhariṣyāmi yuṣmān asmād duruttarāt । katham uttārayiṣyāmi lokaṃ saṃsārasāgarāt ।। etāni cānyāni ca bodhisattvāḥ kurvanti karmāṇy avipannasattvāḥ ।
parārthacaryāviṣaye carantaḥ kṛpānubhūtāḥ svasukhānurāgāḥ ।। anāvṛtadvāram idaṃ niketanaṃ durāvahāṇāṃ bhavaduḥkhapattriṇāṃ । cirāt pramodāyatanī kariṣyate mayā śarīraṃ suhṛdāṃ hitāgame ।। bhavatparitrāṇamaye sukhodaye niyojya kāyaṃ niyataṃ mayāpsyate ।
abhedyam acchedyam ahāryam avyayaṃ niruttaraṃ dharmaśarīram avraṇam ।। amitrabhūtaṃ yadi mitrasād imaṃ kaliṃ kariṣyāmi na kāyasaṃjñakam । vidhakṣyate vipratisāravahninā mano viniśvāsaśikhena me ciram ।। gataviklavā bhavanto madīyam udgataprāṇaṃ śarīraṃ plavam ivālambyānyonyasaṃsaktikayā vārivegavaśena yena vātena vā digbhāgena sthalam upagamya parṇamūlaphalajalādibhir yāpayantaḥ parasparam avipannasauhṛdāḥ karmasvakatāvalambino lokasvabhāvam avekṣamāṇā vinītavivādaśokadainyāḥ kāryāvasānam āgamayata । sukham anubhūya duḥkham apy anubhūyate । saṃpattim apy upāsya vipattir upāsyate । saṃsāracārakāvacarāṇāṃ hi etad eva paryāptaṃ vyasanam ataḥ pratikaṣṭatarāṇy apy atra kṛcchrāṇy āsādyante śrutimanovidāhinī । na hy enam anupatan kaś cit sukhī nāma । prabalānilākulānalajvālākalāpamadhyagatasyānuktasiddhaṃ dāhaduḥkham । tṛṣṇāvidheyamanasāṃ cābhimukhaḥ parābhava utsaṅgagatāni sarvadainyāny āsannavartī paribhavo bhayam upari vyavasthitam abhito vipralambhavaikṛtāni । saṃkṣepataḥ sarvam aśivajālam upagṛhya tṛṣṇā naram upabadhnāti । sa ca madviyogadainyāvakāśo na hṛdi karaṇīyaḥ । īdṛśo hi lokasvabhāvo viyogaduḥkhānugatā eva hi priyajanasaṃyogāḥ ।
dīrghakālaparicayād dṛḍhasnehanibaddhāny api sauhṛdāni kṣaṇena viśliṣyanti । prāṇināṃ viparyāsaś caiṣa cetasaḥ priyo ayaṃ mameti । dṛśyante kāraṇāntaraviparyayāt parivartamānāni priyāpriyāṇi jīvaloke । tasmān na paratantreṣv apariniṣpannasvabhāveṣu prakṛtibhedavartiṣu vipralambhapadasthāneṣu kṣaṇavipariṇāmalolaśīleṣu śokāyāsamayeṣu priyasamāgameṣv abhiniviśyātmā khedayitavyaḥ । tatra sukhaṃ dhairyam eva paruṣāṇām āpatsv avalambo bhavati viṣādam avadhīrayati śokam uparuṇaddhi vighnayati āpadam āpatantīṃ prajñānasahitaṃ ca tad evābhimatam artham ānayati । śokānivṛttis tu niṣprayojanam āśrayaṃ saṃtāpayati kṛtyam antarayati kāntim ācchinatti pratibhānam āyāsayaty āsannasnehaduḥkhaṃ suhṛjjanaṃ dharmārthayaśaḥsukhāni copahanti । matkṛtam anupaśyadbhis tu bhavadbhiḥ puṇyeṣv ādaraḥ karaṇīyaḥ । puṇyam eva hi prāṇinām ihāmutra ca niratyayo bandhur āpatsu viṣādī sahāyaḥ pātheyam ayatnavāhyaṃ pradīpas tamasi prapāteṣu saṃkramaṃ bhayasthāneṣv ārakṣā maṅgalam advaidhasiddham atyantikaṃ siddhaṃ sūpacaraḥ svāmī parāyaṇam āpadgatānām āyatanam avipariṇāmināṃ sukhānāṃ kṣetraṃ diśāvidiśāntavyāpināṃ yaśasāṃ ākaraḥ praśaṃsānām anabhibhūtaṃ vaiśāradyam । puṇyāvaṣṭhambhād eva ca puruṣo duravagāhe api sukham avagāhate । paralokakāntāre viṣādapadasthāne api nāma maraṇasamaye na viṣīdanti puṇyakarmāṇaḥ । kaṇṭakapracayakarkaśāny api janmadurgāṇi prāyeṇākṣatāḥ saṃcaranti puṇyabalinaḥ । puṇyair eva cākhilajagaddhitasukhādhyāśayapravṛttivistīrṇām ākarṣayanti sakalabhuvanādhipatyābhiṣekamahatīṃ sarvalokasādhāraṇāṃ tāthāgatīṃ guṇasamṛddhiṃ prāg eva pratanusukhānavakāśādīnavāṃ pracurajanamanovikāriṇīm anantaduḥkhabāṇasaṃnipātadūṣitām āyāsinīm iha paratra ca bāliśānāṃ pratikṣaṇavyayānubandhādūṣitām anekarūpavairakṛtānuṣaṅgadāruṇāṃ bhavabhogamayīm aśivām akhilāṃ viparītasukhābhiniveśakhalāṃ saṃpattisaṃjñāntaritāṃ vipattim akāraṇabhraṃśamanovidāhinīm ity alam iti prasaṅgenātipatati । kāryakālaś caramasaṃdeśo ayaṃ bhadramukhā ity uktvā bodhisattvo muhūrtam ekāgramano babhūva । nivāryamāṇo api śataiḥ suhṛdbhir bāṣpāmbuvisyandivilocanāntaiḥ । sādhuḥ svadehāśrayaṇīm apekṣāṃ tatyāja lokavyasanopataptaḥ ।।
ārtasvarair aviratair avibhaktavarṇais teṣāṃ viṣādapariluptamanaḥsthitīnām । āpūryamāṇasalilapradarāntarālaḥ saṃcukṣubhe bhṛśataraṃ lavaṇāmburāśiḥ ।। bodhisattvo api mahāsattva iti praṇidhim upabṛmhayām āsa śāntaye sarvasattvānām । prāg evānyā parimitasukhapratyayapratyapāyā ।
puṇyād asmān na ca śamasukhaṃ prārthaye projjhya lokān ।। tṛṣṇātoye madanakaluṣe krodhasaṃsarpisarpe । puṇyād asmād aham aśaraṇaṃ kṛtsnam uttārayeyam ।। tyaktāpekṣaḥ sucaritaśatopārjite api svadehe ।
svāṃ śokārtivyathitahṛdayaḥ prāṇināṃ tāraṇāya ।। atha śuśruvire giraḥ śubhāḥ suravidyādharayakṣarakṣasām । iti citramanoharāśrayāḥ patitās tasya guṇopasaṃhitāḥ ।। puṇyābhyāsaviśeṣapuṇyamahatām āścaryarūpasthitiḥ ।
bata kṛpā nāpekṣate svāśrayam ।। kīrtyā candramayūkhadhautakumudacchāyā । janmāvaskarakardame sphuradurukleśakrimivyākule ।। divyodyānadrumebhyaḥ kusumam avirataṃ taccharīre papāta ।
vyābhugnopāntamadhyaiḥ kuvalayamṛdubhis taṃ bhujaṅgāḥ praṇemuḥ ।। lakṣmyā samālabdham iva prakāmaṃ pramṛṣṭacāmīkaracāruvarṇam । samudgataprāṇam api prasannaṃ rarāja tat tasya vibhoḥ śarīram ।। ālambya plavam iva te atha taccharīraṃ bāṣpāmbuvyatikarapāṭalāntanetrāḥ ।
utterur makarakarakṣatormicakraṃ tasyaiva praṇidhibalāśrayāt samudram ।। cakāra jagatāṃ kṛpāparigatāmalādhyāśayaḥ । samagrabhuvanopakārakaraṇaikavīre jine ।। vaco avitathavādinaḥ śrutirasāyanaṃ śrūyatām ।
bhavādhvani nirāśraye vyasanakaṇṭakāndhācite ।। iti śrīsārthavāhajātakaṃ samāptam ।। paraduḥkhaduḥkhitāḥ svajīvitam api nāpekṣante sādhavaḥ । tadyathānuśrūyate ।
bodhisattvo anyatamaṃ svakulakramāgataṃ mahīmaṇḍalaṃ samanuśaśāsa । tasyārthijanamanoharair aviṣamapravṛttimadhuratarair anatikrāntakālābhilaṣitaiḥ phalāśākārpaṇyopaśamasvacchaśobhair vibhavavisargair lokān saṃtarpayataḥ sarvaṃdada ity evaṃ yathārthaṃ nāma prathitam āsīt । jagaddhitādhānasamutsukatvāt sa rājyabhāraṃ bibharāṃ babhūva । kṣitīśvaraḥ pūrvakṛtānavadyapuṇyaprabhāvopanataṃ krameṇa ।। na tasya kiṃpākaphalopamāś calā mano manovibhramamātrabhadrikāḥ ।
svabhāgadheyopanatā vibhūtayo babandhur āryaprakṛter mahātmanaḥ ।। pariśramas tasya babhūva yautako mahākṛpādhīnamater mahīpateḥ । prabhutvam āsīj jagatāṃ tv abādhithaṃ vibhūtisaṃbhogasukheṣu bhūriṣu ।। na tasya mātsaryatamo'vaguṇṭhanaṃ babhūva gātreṣv api mānasaṃ yadā ।
tadā kathaivoparatāsukhāgate tṛṇopame śokanibandhane dhane ।। taṃ kila mahātmānam anyatamaḥ pārthivo atṛptaḥ svarājyaśriyā parityaktadharmayaśāḥ sukhasādhanopāyadāruṇaḥ svarājyād uccālayitum upacakrame । saṃprāpya bhogān mahato apy anāryāḥ panthānam āryācaritaṃ vilaṅghya । tṛṣṇāparītāḥ karuṇātmakeṣu sādhuṣv api krodhaviṣaṃ vamanti ।।
bhaiṣajyavṛkṣā iva ye kadā cit kva cit kathaṃ cij jagato hitāya । bhavanti tān apy upataptacittāḥ krodhāgninā kāpuruṣā dahanti ।। kurvīta ko nāma manuṣya āryaḥ sacetanas teṣu manaḥpradoṣam । yeṣāṃ yaśobhiḥ kumudāvadātair udbhāsitānīva digantarāṇi ।।
atha dharaṇirajobhiḥ śārikākaṇṭhadhūmrais turagakhuranipātaprodgataiś chādayan kham । sa nṛpatir upatasthe mattamātaṅgasainyair upavanatarupūgān ārujan meghanīlān ।। udadhir iva yugānte plāvayaṃl lokam antarlulitamakarapucchacchinnacañcattaraṅgaḥ । sa nṛpabalasamūho nagnanistriṃśapattrasphuritaravimayūkhas tatpuraṃ saṃrurodha ।।
upanatam api puṇyair vipralambhāvasānaṃ dhig anupaśamakāri śrīsukhaṃ pārthivānām । piśitam iva vipūti kravyabhugmaṇḍalānāṃ yad iha bhavati puṃsāṃ vairavairasya mūlam ।। atha bodhisattvaḥ prāg eva viditaviṣayadoṣavairavairaḥ saṃrambhavipralabhādyanarthabhūyiṣṭhaṃ rājyam atimanyamānaḥ svasukhasaṃbhogābhiṣvaṅgadainyānupakliṣṭamānasaś cintayāṃ babhūva । dhig astv anāryaṃ viṣayāśrayaṃ sukhaṃ samīraṇoddhūtalatāntacañcalam ।
upāsate yatra nibaddhamānasā narā daśāṃ bandhujanopatāpinīm ।। dānaprasrutisiktadantamusalakrūradvipendrākulam । rakṣed akṣatacāriṇī yadi kṛpā māteva māṃ nāpadi ।। tāṃ vāñched bhramaropagītakusumāṃ ko vadhyamālām iva ।
