prāg eva vyasanāturasya jagato yo ahaṃ hitāyodyataḥ ।। rājye aparo yadi mama praṇayaṃ karoti pūjyo mayā nanu viśeṣata eva rājā । rājyāśrayaṃ khalu parārtham ahaṃ bibharmi saṃkleśabhāram imam āyataduḥkhahetum ।। atithir iva yato ayaṃ mānanīyo narendro madupahitavibhūtiprārthanākṛṣṭacetāḥ ।
upacitakuśalatvāc cānukampāviśeṣāt suta iva vinayārthaṃ ko atra kopāvakāśaḥ ।। unmocayaty eva balāc ca yo māṃ rājyābhidhānād vyasanapratānāt । yady atra kuryāṃ manasaḥ prakopaṃ pāpo aparaḥ ko atha mayā samaḥ syāt ।। rājyasya doṣāvayave niveśaṃ prakhyāpayan hanti yaśaḥsukhāni ।
mām arthataḥ śikṣayate narendro rājyābhidhāne tamasi bhramantam ।। tyaktavyam etena ca kāraṇena kṣitīśvaraśrīsukham ātmakāmaiḥ । yad atra saktasya janasya vairabhayaprasaṅgāḥ śirasi sphuranti ।। yo vāham utsṛjya tapovanāni nirantarāyāṇy abhitaḥ śivāni ।
gṛhābhidhānaṃ bhayam āvasāmi nārhāmi nāhaṃ vyasanāny amūni ।। tat svastirājyadyutivistarebhyo naikavyalīkāśrayadāruṇebhyaḥ । yāsyāmi śāntāni vanāny ato ahaṃ vivekajaprītinibandhanāni ।। kalyāṇamitraṃ yata eva rājā mamādya naiṣkramyasukhodayāya ।
kalyāṇam evāstv anayo apy ato asya sabandhumitrasya śaracchatāni ।। pratyāsannopatāpām anuvahasi vṛthā bhaṅginīṃ kiṃ nayājñām । śaṅke daurjanyam itthaṃ mama nṛpatir ayaṃ kṣāpayiṣyaty ayatnaḥ ।। vane vatsyāmīti praśamasukhasaṃbhogasubhage ।
prasiddhās te diṣṭyā kṣitipatim imaṃ prāpya na cirāt ।। iti viniścitya bodhisattvo janmāntarābhyastanaiṣkramyasukhābhyudayaparicayo mṛga iva vāgurāvarodhanirgamopalambhodbhūtapramodaḥ samapanītarājyaśrīsūcakālaṃkāravibhramakāyabhāralaghuviviktavigrahaḥ parair aparijñātatapovanagamanaprayojanaḥ saṃrūḍhapraṇayaviśrambhasnehabahumānaniratyayaṃ ca bandhuvargaṃ svapuṇyabalāvaṣṭambhopanatasukhopabhogyāṃ ca rājalakṣmīṃ paryuṣitopabhogamalinamlānakusumabandhanām iva srajaṃ parityajyānytamad viviktam āśramapadam alaṃcakāra । śākhākaraiḥ svakusumābharaṇābhirāmaiḥ । prāpto amṛtaṃ nṛpasukhair anavāptapūrvam ।।
yāny eva śokaparidevamukhāni loke kāmātmanām anucitopaśamotsavānām । tāny eva nāma dadhati praśamapriyāṇāṃ prītiṃ nirāmiṣasukhapraṇayānavadyām ।। saṃvījitaḥ prativinodya śarīrakhedam । saṃvegam eva manasi kṣitipaḥ pupoṣa ।।
sarvātmanā daśasu dikṣu tathāgatebhyaḥ । mūle taroḥ kṣitipatir niṣasāda madhye ।। sa khedito antaḥpurasundarīṇāṃ saṃkleśapakṣānuguṇair vilāsaiḥ । viviktasaṃbhogasukhāny araṇyāny ālokya viśrānta iva kṣitīśaḥ ।।
parisravannirjharavāridhārāprakṣālitaśyāmaśilātalāni । sānūni paśyan sa mahīdharāṇām ayatnaramyāṇi mudaṃ jagāma ।। āliṅgitān puṣpabharālasābhiḥ snehād iva prāṇasamāṃl latābhiḥ । mahīruhān bhūripalāśanīlān ālokya reme sa mahīmahendraḥ ।।
akarkaśaśyāmakaśerukāṇi bhramaddvirephāhatapuṣkarāṇi । nirīkṣamāṇaḥ sa nṛpo abhireme sarāṃsi pāṭhīnakulākulāni ।। vivekajaprītisukhānukūlāṃ nisargaramyāṃ sa vanāntabhūmim । nirīkṣamāṇaḥ kṣitipaḥ praharṣaṃ jagāma saṃśāntamanovikāraḥ ।।
udīkṣya saṃsaktaśikhaṇḍikekāmano'bhirāmāṇi sa kānanāni । anekasaṃkleśaviṣopadagdhāṃ nṛpaśriyaṃ bhūmipatir jagarhe ।। kvāsau viparyāsasukhābhimānaprasaṅgajihmā kṣitipālalakṣmīḥ । kva caiva cetovinibandhanāni śāntāny araṇyāśrayiṇāṃ sukhāni ।।
anartharāgāśrayadūṣitāya namo astu tasmai kṣayiṇe sukhāya । viṣajya yasmin manasaḥ pravṛttiṃ kṛpāspadatvaṃ viduṣāṃ vrajanti ।। kṛtaparikaraśrīsaṃbhogāḥ praśāntarayoddhavāḥ । kṣititalapatiḥ paśyaṃl lebhe ratiṃ sa nirāmiṣām ।।
hṛdayam asatāṃ śānte araṇye ratiṃ katham eṣyati । viṣayavimukhaḥ prītiṃ bheje parāṃ vijane vane ।। na khalu hṛdayaṃ no jñānārthaṃ haranti vibhūtayaḥ । bhavati tu satāṃ pūrvābhyāsān matiḥ praguṇā śubhe ।।
kusumaśabalair viśvākhātais taraṅgitapādapāḥ । manasi na mudaṃ kasyādadhyuḥ śivā vanarājayaḥ ।। viṣayamarutā vyādhūtānāṃ hatopaniṣatsukham । vrajati tu manaḥ sadyaḥ śāntiṃ kukāryasamākulam ।।
athānyatamo brāhmaṇo dāridryaduḥkhābhyāhatas tatpratīkāracikīrṣayā mandotsāho api bodhisattvam ekam ārtāyanam avagamya tadviṣayāntam upagacchan mārgaparibhraṃśaparyākulātmā tatas tataḥ paribhraman kṣudduḥkhopaglapitatanur adhvaklamaviklavāvidheyagurutaracaraṇavigrahas tad āśramapadam āsasāda । dṛṣṭvā cainaṃ bodhisattvaś cirābhyāgatasnigdhabāndhavasnehātiriktavātsalyapeśalayā pibann iva dṛṣṭyā pratyudgamyābhivādya ca kṛtapratisaṃmodanam āgamanaprayojanaṃ paryapṛcchat । brāhmaṇo abravīt । yaḥ sarvado nāma bhuvi prasiddho yathārthanāmā naralokapālaḥ । kīrtyā samāhūta ivāsmi tasya prāptas tam ārtāyanam īkṣamāṇaḥ ।। trātā sa eva vyasanāturāṇāṃ vanīpakānāṃ sa ca bandhur ekaḥ ।
tam eva caikaṃ vyapadiśya sādhum anyatra maunavratam eti vāṇī ।। tat tasya vacanaṃ śrutvā sa kṛpāpeśalāśayaḥ । ācakampe mahāsattvas tadduḥkhapavanāhataḥ ।। atha sa mahātmā dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niśvasya taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ provāca ।
upāyaś cintyatām anyo dvija duḥkhopaśāntaye । bhraṣṭaiśvaryaḥ sa bhūpālas tapase vanam āśritaḥ ।। atha sa brāhmaṇaḥ samīhitārthapratyāśāpraṇayabhaṅgadainyākrāntamānasaḥ sahasā pṛthivyāṃ nipapāta paraṃ ca saṃmoham upajagāma । āśāparyastadhairyāṇi hṛdayāni prasaṅginām ।
dehināṃ moham āyānti hetunā yena kena cit ।। atha bodhisattvas taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣiñcya pratilabdhasaṃjñaṃ samāśvāsayann abravīt । asty anyo api pratīkāro bhavadāśāsamṛddhaye । ahaṃ sarvaṃdado rājā mā śucas tvam iha dvija ।।
sarvaṃdado nāma kathaṃ kadā vā yasya svadehe api manaḥprasaṅgaḥ । yathārthanāmā tv adhunā bhaviṣyāmy ahaṃ tvadabhyāgamanotsavena ।। madrājyapraṇayī rājā māṃ samanveṣate kila । baddhvā māṃ dehy atas tasmai sa tvāṃ samtoṣayiṣyati ।।
anekaduḥkhopanipātakātaraś cirasya tāvad bhavadāśrayād ayam । mamopayogaṃ guṇapakṣasiddhaye śarīrasaṃjñaḥ kalir adya yāsyati ।। jarārujāmṛtyukhalūrikām imāṃ tanuṃ samāśritya sa hanta yo adya me । manoratho brāhmaṇamukhya pūryatāṃ tava prabhāvād abhivāñchitaś ciram ।।
prītir nṛpasya tava cārthaviśeṣasiddhiḥ saṃpatsyate mama ca pāramitāprakarṣaḥ । ekaṃ śarīram atisṛjya vipatparītaṃ paśyotsavātiśayam āpatitaṃ krameṇa ।। evaṃvidhe atithijanapraṇayābhidhāne prītyāgame ca mama kāryasamṛddhihetau । dehe kṛtāntamakarāsyapuṭātithau ca naikopasargavihite vidhir asti ko anyaḥ ।। kāyād asārād aham adya sāraṃ bhavantam āsādya samujjihīrṣuḥ ।
manorathaṃ tat saphalaṃ kuruṣva tvam adya me vipra cirānubaddham ।। evam astv iti pāpātmā pratiśuśrāva sa dvijaḥ । atikramyāryamaryādāṃ lobhopahatamānasaḥ ।। koṭarāntargatavyālaviṣād apy atidāruṇaiḥ ।
viṣayair upataptānāṃ pāpaṃ kiṃ nāma duṣkaram ।। ekaḥ parārthaṃ pradadau svadehaṃ samādade anyaḥ param ātmahetoḥ । aho vikṛṣṭaṃ caritaṃ narāṇāṃ guṇeṣu doṣeṣu ca sādarāṇām ।। taṃ bodhisattvaṃ vinibadhya gāḍhaṃ paścādbhujaṃ cauram iva dvijātiḥ ।
samācakarṣa prakṛtipragalbho nivāryamāṇo vanadevatābhiḥ ।। sākṣād ayaṃ dharma ivāvatīrṇaḥ praśāntavākkāyamanovikāraḥ । dvijādhamenāvinayāvalepakrūreṇa kaṣṭaṃ hriyate maharṣiḥ ।। amī rudantīva vilolapallavāḥ praśastapuṣpāśrumukhā mahīruhāḥ ।
caladdvirephadhvanidīnanisvanā viyujyamānā muninā sumedhasā ।। sudurlabham darśanam asya sarvathā vilocanaprītikarasya dehinām । vilepur ity udgataśokakātarāḥ pragāḍhaśokā munayo vanaukasaḥ ।। ādāya vipro atha tam āryasattvaṃ niḥsādhvasānākuladhīraceṣṭam ।
praveśayām āsa puraṃ sa yasmin mahīpatis tṣṭhati tatsapatnaḥ ।। gajaskandhārūḍhaṃ patim iva surāṇāṃ narapatim । mukhaiḥ śokāyāsastimitagurupakṣmāntanayanaiḥ ।। prāṃśuṃ sumerum iva lakṣaṇaratnacitram ।
dṛṣṭvā nṛpo ripur adhīratayā cakampe ।। tathābhūtaṃ cainam avekṣya sādhvasākulitamatiś cintayām āsa । kṣāmodaro bhujagabhogavilambibāhuḥ । prāpto yuvāpi vinayapratipattidhīraḥ ।।
dharmo avatīrṇa iva vigrahavān kuto ayam ālambavalkaladharo nayanābhirāmaḥ । baddhaś ca nāma ca na dainyaviṣādavaśyas tejonidhiḥ praśamam udgiratīva cāyam ।। atha sa brāhmaṇādhamas taṃ rājānam abravīt । jayatu jayatu mahārājo diṣṭyā vardhase । yo asau tava pratyanīko rājā kenāpi prayojanenāraṇyam anupraviśya tāpasanepathyāvacchādito daurātmyaṃ kim apy ārebhe । sa eṣa mayā balātkāraṃ tvatpriyacikīrṣayā baddhvā mīna iva sphurann ānītas tad atra devaḥ pramāṇam iti । atha sa rājā tat tasya pāpakarmaṇaḥ karmāsaṃbhāvayann avocad enam । mā tāvad bhoḥ । śaktaḥ śaktimatāṃ varaḥ karikaravyālambibāhudrumaḥ । tat tvaṃ brūhi parābhavanti na mṛgāḥ siṃhaṃ sphuratkesaram ।।
sa tasmai rājñe yathābhūtam āviścakāra । dhik tvām iti ca nirbhartsitaḥ kopakaluṣayā dṛṣṭyā tena rājñā parāṃ vrīḍām āpannaḥ । svayam eva vimucya bandhanāni kṣitipaḥ so atha yathāsukhaṃ nṛparṣim upaveśya tam āsane mahārhe bahumānānatavigraho jagāda । guṇabhaktitayātimānuṣaṃ te nṛpa karmātiśayāvadānam etat । prathayanti surāsurapradhānā bahumānaślatham ānataiḥ śirobhiḥ ।। yadi rañjayituṃ prajāḥ samartho nṛpa rājety abhidhānasaṃniveśaḥ ।
guṇaratnanidhe tvam eva rājā viguṇo rañjayituṃ jagan na śaktaḥ ।। anuśādhi yathā purā puraṃ svaṃ vayam ājñāpravaṇā bhavadvidhānām । vinayād vyasanaṃ ca naḥ kṣamethāḥ skhalati proṣitalocanaḥ same api ।। jātaprasādam atha taṃ nṛpatiṃ viditvā pātrīkṛtaṃ sucaritasya sa bodhisattvaḥ ।
śiṣyaṃ vinītam iva gauravabhāranamraṃ provāca nīlajaladastanayitnughoṣaḥ ।। āyur nṛṇām acirakālavināśi tāvat taptopalodaraniṣikta ivāmbubinduḥ । saṅgāḥ priyaiḥ saha sadaiva viyogatiktāḥ saṃpattayo vipariṇāmaviṣāviṣahyāḥ ।। kāmā muhūrtavitathābhiniveśarāmāḥ kiṃpākapādapaphalapratimopabhogāḥ ।
naikāntarāyavirasaṃ sabhayaṃ savairaṃ rājyaṃ pramādavadhabandhanimittabhūtam ।। tasmād vipākamadhurāṇi kuruṣva nityaṃ karmāṇi sajjanamanovinibandhanāni । śokāśrukātaramukhās tu vipākakāle yeṣāṃ bhavanti puruṣāḥ prajahīhi tāni ।। vairāyāsaviṣādadainyakalahadvāraiḥ parapratyayaiḥ ।
puṣpālambakadambapādapavanaśyāmopakaṇṭhāḥ śivāḥ ।। hariṇakulaviluptasnigdhaśaṣpottarīyā nipatitasitapuṣpā dyaur ivālakṣyatārā । apaharati balān me mānasaṃ kānanāntakṣitir uparatarājyaprārthanāvipralambham ।। sthiravanagamanāśayaṃ viditvā nṛpatir asāv atha taṃ viśuddhasattvam ।
apahṛtahṛdayo guṇais tadiyair vanagamanābhimukhaḥ kilāvatasthe ।। avagamitamanāś ca bodhisattvaḥ kṣitipatinā vinayānatena tena । uparataviṣayaspṛho api ceto vanagamanād vinivartayāṃ babhūva ।। vana iva bhavane api bodhisattvā viṣayasukhavyasanāparītasattvāḥ ।
munaya iva vanāntavāsanimnāḥ praśamarasaikavihāriṇo bhavanti ।। bhavana iva vane api sādhavas te jagadudayaikanibandhanaprayogāḥ । svatanum api parārtham utsṛjanti praṇayijanapraṇayaṃ na khaṇḍayanti ।। ata iha bhavanaṃ vanaṃ ca tulyaṃ jagadupajīvyavibhūtivistarāṇām ।
avikalabhuvanopakārapārapraṇayakṛtavyavasāyamānasānām ।। tena dattaṃ samādāya svarājyaṃ lokasārathiḥ । dhanaṃ rājā sa viprāya vāñchitātyadhikaṃ dadau ।। tyaktvā vairavikāraduḥsahataraṃ krodhābhidhānaṃ viṣam ।
cakre taccaraṇāmbujapraṇayinīm uṣṇīṣamālāṃ kṣaṇāt ।। tasmin gate nijapuraṃ vinayaprapanne saṃprāpya rājyam arihīnam udārapuṇyaḥ । dharmeṇa kīrtidhavalāmbudhiphenamālāvelādukūlalalitāṃ pṛthivīṃ śaśāsa ।। caritam atigatopamānaśobhaṃ na hi vibhavo asty anugantum īśvarāṇām ।
mama kṛpaṇamates tathāpi caitat kṛtam atisāhasam ātmano hitāya ।। kuśalam upacitaṃ kṛpātmakānāṃ caritam idaṃ vinibadhya yan mayādya । bhavatu bhuvanaśāntaye tad āśu jvalatu tathāgataśāsanaṃ tataś ca ।। iti sarvaṃdadajātakam ।।
paraduḥkhakātarā devarājyam apy avadhīrayanti sādhavaḥ ।। bodhisattvabhūtaḥ kila bhagavān svapuṇyaparipākaviśeṣopanatam amarapurādhipatyam kārayām āsa । naparidyūtahṛdayena sarvalokātiśayināpi mahimnā kevalaṃ puṇyānām avandhyaphalam āviṣkurvann amarapuranivāsināṃ cānugrahāya ।। na sa svarge reme prakṛtiramaṇīye api bhagavān । parārthaprāgbhārā paramavidhurā svāduvidhurā ।।
kṛpaṇamanasāṃ yad vā mano bahu manyate । na viṣayasukheṣv āsthaṃ ceto mahaty api rakṣyate ।। sa kadā cij jambūdvīpam avalokayan dadarśa [!] evaṃ lokam aśakyapratīkāravyādhiduḥkhopaplutaṃ viṣamavirasakṛtavaidyasāmarthyaṃ samaraṇam āvarjja vyavasāyaviklavaṃ romanthamānam iva piśitāśanair ihaiva narakaduḥkhāny anubhavantaṃ vismṛtasnehabandhumitrasuhṛcchaucācāraprayojanam ।। kṛtāntakarmānta iva pravṛttas tadā sa rogāntarakalpatulyaḥ ।
aśakyarūpapratikārabhīmo mahātyayo vyādhikṛto vikāraḥ ।। vikṣiptāṅgāḥ kṣititalarajoguṇṭhitoddhastakeśāḥ । madhukaragaṇair mārga āsannapātāḥ ।। sṛkkāntapratibaddhaśuṣkavirasaśleṣmānanā bhīṣaṇāḥ ।
ke cit pūrvakṛtaṃ ninindur aśubhaṃ karmābhisaṃdhisthiram ।। kvathitapiśitarandhraprodvamatpūyadhārā malinavikṛtadehāḥ ke cid aprekṣaṇīyāḥ । krimikulapariluptaprāyabāhūdaroruśravaṇanayananāsāḥ prārthayante sma kālam ।। rūkṣakṣāmavidāritānanapuṭāḥ pretā ivāyāsinaḥ ।
vīkṣantaḥ sarasāṃ payāṃsi viviśuḥ ke cit kṛtāntālayam ।। dūṣīkāpaṭalaniruddhalocanāntā durgandhā bahalamalopaliptagātrāḥ । anye tu klamaśithilāśrayā rujānām ājagmur nilayanatāṃ prabandhinīnām ।। śmaśruvrātāḥ pathiṣu kṛpaṇāḥ klāntakāyāḥ śayānāḥ ।
vyāvṛttāsyā vipadam avaśāḥ pratyapadyanta tīvrām ।। tasya tad atidāruṇam ālokya lokavyasanaṃ mahat kāruṇyam udapādi । atha sa mahāsattvas tena sattvopadraveṇa vyathitamanāḥ sutarām abhivardhitānukampākampitaḥ pitevaikaputravyasanam asahamānaś cintām apede ।। itthaṃ gatānāṃ ka ivābhyupāyaḥ syād āmayocchittisukhaḥ prajānām । apīha lokatrayabāndhavānāṃ tathāgatānām anṛṇo bhaveyam ।।
api nāma bhaven mama pratijñā sakalā lokahitaprayogasiddhyai । api mānuṣajanmaduḥkhabhājo vyasanebhyaḥ parimokṣam aśnuvīran ।। api nāma na bodhisattvanāmavyapadeśaṃ vitathaṃ samudvaheyam । api sarvavidām agarhaṇīyāṃ dadhad ājñām animittavatsalānām ।।
bhavaduḥkhaśilīmukhakṣatānām api mateva piteva ca prajānām । aham eva parāyaṇaṃ paraṃ syāṃ bhavaduḥkhāmburayapratīrabhūtaḥ ।। kālāher āsyakośaṃ sakalajagadanugrāsasaṃbhogabhīmam । prāṇatyāgānurāgaṃ praṇayasukhakaraṃ bhūtabhṛtyai karomi ।।
vyavasāyam iti jñātvā tasyātyadbhutakarmaṇaḥ । tadviyogābhiśaṅkārtā vicukruśur athāmarāḥ ।। kṛpālo duḥkhitān asmān parityajya kva yāsyasi । viṣamasthān iva pitā vatsalo bālaputrakān ।।
saddharmasalilotsekair vardhayan pādapān iva । asmān anāgasas tyaktvā mā yāsīḥ priyadarśana ।। viṣayāsvādacapalair hṛtān indriyavājibhīḥ । svāmin māsmān parityākṣīḥ prapātāntānucāriṇaḥ ।।
praṇāmalolānatamaulibandhanān pragāḍhaśokopanipātakātarān । athāmarān aśrupariplutekṣaṇān sa sāntvayann ity avadan marutpatiḥ ।। na me na yuṣmāsv anurāgapeśalaṃ mano na cāyaṃ svahitodayādaraḥ । vikāsinīnāṃ vipadāṃ mukhe sthitaṃ jagat paritrātum ayaṃ tu niścayaḥ ।।
tad apramādaḥ kriyatāṃ sa eva vo dhruvaṃ samārtāyanatām upeṣyati । visaṃvadanty eva samāgamāḥ priyair nipātaramyāḥ pariṇāmadāruṇāḥ ।। sthitvāpi kālam atulaṃ vividhopabhogasaṃbhogavistarasukhais tridaśādhivāse । karmakṣayād vinipatanti surāḥ smarantaḥ saṃvartakānilahatā iva kalpavṛkṣāḥ ।।
mandākinīm api vigāhya sahāpsarobhir unnidrahemakamalocchuritopakaṇṭhām । kṣārodakāṃ jvalanadarbhakukūlakūlāṃ nighnāḥ punar yadi ca vaitaraṇīṃ bhajante ।। ko nāma teṣu matimān svamano nidadhyād utkṣepaṇīyakusumāvayavopameṣu । svargopabhogajaniteṣu sukheṣu yeṣām anteṣv apāyavaḍavāmukhasaṃniveśaḥ ।।
kalpadrumopavanabhūmiṣu naikaratnaprodbhāsyamānatatatalpaśilātalāsu । sākaṃ priyābhir anubhūya sukhāni bhūyas tīkṣṇāsipattravanamadhyagatā bhavanti ।। saṃbhrāntabālahariṇekṣaṇacañcalāni vibhrāntakālapariṇāmakarāṇi buddheḥ । yad dhīndriyārthaparibhogasukhāni tasmād yatnaṃ surāḥ kuruta puṇyaparigrahāya ।।
edhobhir agnaya iva praśamaṃ vrajanti kāmāgnayo na viṣayair viṣapānakalpaiḥ । tasmād upāddhvam anavadyasukhābhirāmāṃ tāthāgatīṃ pratipadaṃ vyasanopaśāntyai ।। gaṇopaghrātānāṃ paraśubhir ivotkṛttavapuṣām । kariṣyāmo muktvā surabhavanasaṃbhogavasitām ।।
mama jagadupakāraprārthanāsaṃniveśaḥ । na khalu kuśalavighnaṃ kartum arhanti santaḥ ।। atimānuṣam apy apāsya citraṃ mahimānaṃ kṛpayā vikṛṣyamāṇaḥ । sa tu duḥkhakaro gatau tiraścāṃ paramāryaḥ pratisaṃdadhe mahātmā ।।
karuṇāmṛtapeśalāśayānāṃ svasukhāsaṅgaviviktamānasānām । prabhavā iva kalpapādapānām udayā lokahitāya sajjanānām ।। vinayānataratnamauliraśmicchuritās taṃ na marudgaṇapraṇāmāḥ । manujātisukhaṃ samāpatantaṃ sthirasattvaṃ vinivartayāṃ babhūvuḥ ।।
virahavyasanopatāpadīnair nayanair bāṣpataraṅgadhūsarāntaiḥ । dayitāḥ karuṇaṃ tam īkṣamāṇāḥ śucisattvaṃ na nivartayāṃ babhūvuḥ ।। svajaneṣu na tasya sānukampaṃ na mano dakṣiṇa eva sa prakṛtyā । avagamya garīyasīṃ tathāpi prakṛtiṃ śvā sa tathā cakāra sādhuḥ ।।
sa hitāvahitā rujāturāṇāṃ himavanmerugurur guruḥ prajānām । puruṣātiśayo guṇaprakarṣān niyataṃ dūrataraṃ samutpapāta ।। vyavasyanti prāptuṃ salilaphalamūlānilabhujaḥ । tiraścāṃ sābhāgyaṃ sa jagadupakārārtham agamat ।।
tathāgatena prāptā bhavagatisamākṣepavaśitā । tathā hy abhūt janmavyasanaśamanāyaiva jagatām ।। svakāmakārānuvidhāyinīm śriyam paṭāntalagnām hutabhukśikhām iva । na marṣayanti vyasanāturān janān dṛṣṭvā mahāntaḥ karuṇānibandhanāḥ ।।
tasyopapattisamakālam athoccacāra lokaṃ sphuran dhvanir iti śravaṇopakārī । yaḥ pāpy ayaṃ kuru puro bhajanaṃ ca tasya māṃsāsṛjau samupayujya śivaṃ bhajadhvam ।। śrutvātha dhvanim atimānuṣaṃ manuṣyāḥ sāṃhatyasvaritam upetya taṃ pradeśam । ālokya kṣitidharapīvarātmabhāvaṃ taṃ sādhuṃ kṣamiṇam abhīyur udviṣāṇāḥ ।।
āghūrṇasphuṭitakhaḍganiśātapāṇīn dṛṣṭvā tān abhipatato javena gatvā । hāheti sphuṭavirasaṃ vilepur uccaiḥ pratyastapraśithilamaulayaḥ suraughāḥ ।। māṃ dṛṣṭvā ghanavipulāyatātmabhāvaṃ śrutvā vā surapuravāsināṃ pralāpān । na kaś cit pratihatamānaso vasāsṛgmoko ayaṃ kṣaṇam iti so abhavad vikārī ।।
tān paurān suhṛda ivāvalokya tasya prītir yā manasi manasvino jṛmbhate । tām eva kṣitidharasāradhīḥ sa mene paryāptaṃ phalam atiduṣkarasya tasya ।। lokānām abhilaṣitopakāramyaṃ matvāsāv upacitamāṃsam ātmabhavam । ekāntavyasananipātalakṣyabhūte saṃsāre apy abhiratim ābabandha sādhuḥ ।।
ye dhvastāḥ parahitasaṃvidhānaśūnyās taddehāḥ kṣaṇabhidurā bhavaprabandhe । tān manye sa parigaṇayya śailatuṅgān cchuddhyaiva svatanum upādadhe mahātmā ।। taṃ matvā vitatavikāram eva dhairyāt te tīkṣṇais tarum iva cicchiduḥ kuṭhāraiḥ । niḥśaṅkā galitakṛpāśivair manobhiḥ so apy āsīt tarur iva cāpanītamanyuḥ ।।
tadraktavyatirekapāṭalāgrahastās tam khaḍgair araya ivāpare vicakruḥ । so apy āsīd abhimatakāryasaṃprasiddhyā prītyaiva sphuṭahṛdayo viśuddhakarmā ।। susrāva kṣatajam athāsya khaḍgadhārāc chedebhyaḥ sphuṭakaradhīrapuṣpatāmram । saṃprāptaghanasamaye vicitrasānor vindhyādrer jalam iva dhātunirjharebhyaḥ ।।
cakṣāra vraṇamukhakandarebhyo yat tasya kṣatajam iva kṣatāśayasya । tenohur ghanapariṇāhaphenapuñjā viṣṭabdhā vipulasitavīcayaḥ sravantyaḥ ।। tat tasya praṇidhibalāvalambinīnām āśānāṃ katham api pūraṇāt sucetaḥ । saṃprāpte apy amrapure śarīrabhedāt prāmodyaṃ niratiśayopamaṃ babhāra ।।
dadhvāna prapatadasṛkkadeharandhre vicchinne paraśutīkṣṇadhārayāsya । pratyantajvalanaśikhāvalīḍhasānoḥ kuñjeṣu drutam iva kāncanaṃ sumeroḥ ।। tasyograir yugapad itas tataś ca śastrair niḥśaṅkaṃ śakalitakomalāśrayāṅge । vicchinne sahananiviṣṭaśuddhabuddheḥ prītyārdre manasi tirodadhe viṣādaḥ ।।
paricayakṛtamārgās tasya raktapraṇālyo gagaṇaparikhabhūte cchidyamāne śarīre । kṣitidharasaridoghā vistarāṇi pracakrur na ca manasi viṣādo nāpi khedo babhūva ।। apacitataramāṃsāsṛgvasākardamāsu vyapagatabhayaśaṅkās tasya vistāriṇīṣu । tanuvivaratareṣu vyāḍasaṃghā vicerur na ca manasi viṣādo na ca khedo babhūva ।।
yad apahṛtam anāryais tasya māṃsaṃ śarīrād yadi tad apariśeṣaṃ piṇḍitaṃ syāt kathaṃ cit । girim api sa sumeruṃ laṅghayen māṃsarāśir na ca manasi viṣado na ca khedo babhūva ।। kṣayam upayayur aṅgeṣv eva śastrāṇi tasya prakṛtimṛduṣu sādhor akṣatādhyāśayasya । abhirucitaparārthaprītisaṃbhogaśānte na ca manasi viṣādo na ca khedo babhūva ।।
ye cāsya raktair vililepur aṅgā te rejire rogaviṣādamuktāḥ । ye cāpi raktāni papuḥ sarogās te sarvalokāḥ pupuṣur virogāḥ ।। janam apagatarogaṃ vīkṣamāṇasya harṣo manasi bhuvanabandhor labdhagādho babhūva । piśitam anupayogaṃ vīkṣamāṇasya bhūyo apy abhavad aratidolaṃ cañcalaṃ tasya cetaḥ ।।
utkṛttacarmapaṭalasphuṭatāmramāṃso randhrodvamadrudhiraśeṣaviśeṣatāmraḥ । kāyaḥ sa tasya vikṛtaḥ kṛtaniścayasya reje javākusumarāśir ivābhracumbī ।। vicchidyamānaḥ suniśātaśastrais tad duḥkham ekāśrayam īkṣamāṇaḥ । sukhena duḥkhaṃ sa nirācakāra labdhvā paratrātmani caikamatyam ।।
pariṇāmakharā batādhamāyā gatir ātmābhiniveśavāsanāyāḥ । upadigdhadhiyo yayā manuṣyāḥ pitṛbhūteṣv api sādhuṣu skhalanti ।। etasya māṃsaṃ bubhuje kṛpālor yo yaḥ sa sa vyādhim apācakāra । krameṇa kṛcchraṃ jagad uttatāra vipatsamudraṃ tad anena kṛtsnam ।।
atha sarva eva loko vigatanikhilarogopasargas tasmin mahāsattve samupajātapremagauravabahumānaḥ praṇamya śvānaṃ bodhisattvam abravīt ।। aho kṛpābhyāsaviśeṣabhadratā guṇeṣv aho bhaktir apetakalmaṣā । aho parārthapratipattipeśalaṃ tavārya karmedam atītamānuṣam ।। aho jagacchreṣṭhamahādayārdratā aho svasaukhyavyavasāyaniḥspṛhā ।
śubheṣv aho niścayaniścalaṃ mano manasvināṃ bodhipathānupātinām ।। aho batācintyam upāyakauśalam aho parārthe abhirater udāttatā । acintyacaryātiśayāya sādhave namo astu tubhyaṃ jagadekabandhave ।। tvaṃ naḥ pitā yadi pitā tvam ivārthakāmaḥ śāstā tvam eva yadi dharmagurus tvam eva ।
tvam daivataṃ yadi na taj janavādamātram ārtāyanaṃ tu jagataḥ paramaṃ tvam eva ।। tasmād ājñābhiṣekeṇa pavitrayitum arhasi । upadigdham imaṃ lokaṃ yuṣmadāyāsacetasā ।। atha bodhisattvaḥ samupajātaprasādamānasam avagamya tam enam abravīt ।।
pīḍā mameyam iti naivam idaṃ pradhāryaṃ sattvārtham eva gaticakracalasya nityam । pīḍā mamābhavad udīkṣya vipatparītān yuṣmān nirāmayasukhaṃ tv adhunā mano me ।। kṛtyaṃ na me parahitād aparaṃ garīyaḥ saṃsāracārakanibandhanam etad eva । tasmāt kukāryamalinām atilaṅghya caryāṃ matprītaye satatam ātmahitaṃ kurudhvam ।।
lokān imān svakṛtakarmabhujo viditvā mṛtyor aparvaparuṣasya karodarasthān । pāpāny asahyaparitāpaphalodayāni prāṇātyaye api parivarjayituṃ yatadhvam ।। svantāny anāśaramaṇīyaphalapradāni janmāṭavīgahanapathyadanopamāni । puṇyāni saṃcinuta matpratikārabuddhyā kalyāṇamitravacanaṃ hi na laṅghanīyam ।।
iti samanuśiṣya prāṇinas tān mahātmā niśitaparaśudhārājarjaraklāntadehaḥ । avasitakaraṇīyaḥ paryudasyātmabhāvaṃ tam ativikṛtarūpaṃ svargam evāruroha ।। iti jagadupajīvyā uttamaśrīsamudrā vipadaśaninipātavyāhatā vyuṣṭiyogāt । vigatajaladapaṅkavyomaparyantadīrghāḥ śaśina iva mayūkhā lokam uttārayanti ।।
।। iti śrījātakamālāyāṃ śvajātakaṃ tricatvāriṃśattamaṃ samāptam ।।
